#################
# Nomads Events #
#################

# nomads.1   -  99	Reserved for important base events
# nomads.100 - 499	Champions Forge Enclave
# nomads.500 - 999	Heirs of the Khan Origin
# nomads.1000-1500	Forever Cruise Origin
# nomads.1505-1999	Nomadic Paragons
# nomads.2000-2999  The Sacred Path
# nomads.3000-3999  Contracts Functionality
# nomads.4000-4999	Arkship Functionality
# nomads.5000-5999	Civics
# nomads.6000-6999	Contract Events
# nomads.7000-7999	Forgotten Empires
# nomads.8000-8100	Dyson Gun

namespace = nomads

# Fired whenever a new owner is set for a planet, following a war or through trade
# This = Planet scope
# From = Country scope (new owner)
# FromFrom = Country scope (previous owner, if any)
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.1
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			is_planet_class = pc_ark
			has_carrier_flag = nomad_recently_settled_flag
		}
		from = { # Nomads should *never* have planets
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_policy_flag = nomad_total_war_subject
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = { # We split the check for attacker war and defender war into two different if's just to make scripting easier.
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager
				NOMAD = from
				NOMAD_SIDE = defender
				ENEMY = fromfrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = attacker
				TARGET_SYSTEM = root.solar_system
				PLANET = root
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager
				NOMAD = from
				NOMAD_SIDE = attacker
				ENEMY = fromfrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = defender
				TARGET_SYSTEM = root.solar_system
				PLANET = root
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exists = fromfrom
				fromfrom = {
					num_owned_planets > 0
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					from = {
						any_subject = {
							has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
						}
					}
				}
				from = {
					random_subject = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
						}
						save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
						give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
							PLANET = root
							REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
							OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
						}
						nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fromfrom = { is_country_type = default }
				}
				fromfrom.capital_scope.planet = {
					create_rebels = {
						name = random
						ethos = fromfrom
						authority = fromfrom
						civics = fromfrom
						origin = origin_default
						species = fromfrom.species
						flag = random
						effect = {
							set_country_type = default
							set_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
							establish_communications_no_message = from
							establish_communications_no_message = fromfrom
							if = {
								limit = {
									is_homicidal = yes
								}
								change_government = {
									civics = random
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_necrophage
								}
								set_origin = origin_necrophage
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_void_dweller_1
								}
								set_origin = origin_void_dwellers
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_void_dweller_2
								}
								set_origin = origin_void_machines
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_cave_dweller
								}
								set_origin = origin_subterranean
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_robot_cave_dweller
								}
								set_origin = origin_subterranean_machines
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									root.owner = { has_origin = origin_tree_of_life }
									has_trait = trait_hive_mind
								}
								set_origin = origin_tree_of_life
							}

							if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_machine_unit
									root.owner = { is_individual_machine = no }
									NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
								}
								shift_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
								change_government = {
									authority = auth_machine_intelligence
									civics = random
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									has_trait = trait_hive_mind
									NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
								}
								shift_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
								change_government = {
									authority = auth_hive_mind
									civics = random
								}
							}
							save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
							set_subject_of = {
								who = root.owner
								preset = preset_nomad_tributary
							}
							give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
								PLANET = root
								REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
								OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
							}
							nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = { #If we are taking the planet from some weird non default country we create a regular vassal
				create_country= {
					name = random
					ethos = from
					authority = from
					civics = from
					remove_invalid_civics = yes # drop nomad-only civics that aren't valid for this non-nomad vassal
					origin = origin_liberated
					species = from.species
					flag = random
					effect = {
						set_country_type = default
						set_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
						establish_communications_no_message = from
						establish_communications_no_message = fromfrom
						from = {
							every_relation = {
								establish_communications_no_message = prevprev
								add_intel_report = { #Ensuring that they know we are purging pops
									category = economy
									level = 1
									who = prevprev
								}
							}
						}
						set_policy = {
							policy = robot_pop_policy
							option = robot_pops_outlawed
							cooldown = yes
						}
						add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = opinion_liberated_us who = from }
						copy_techs_from = {
							target = from
						}
						copy_traditions_from = {
							target = from
						}
						save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
						set_subject_of = {
							who = from
							preset = preset_nomadic_purger
						}
						random_agreement = {
							add_loyalty = 100
						}
						give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
							PLANET = root
							REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
							OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
						}
						nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
						refresh_species_rights = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exists = fromfrom
				fromfrom = {
					num_owned_planets = 0
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					fromfrom = {
						is_homicidal = no
						is_country_type = default
					}
				}
				from = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_subject = {
								has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
							}
						}
						random_subject = {
							limit = {
								has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
							}
							save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
							fromfrom = {
								set_subject_of = {
									who = root.owner
									preset = preset_nomad_tributary
									allow_instant_negotiation = yes
								}
							}
							give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
								PLANET = root
								REBEL = fromfrom
								OLD_OWNER = event_target:nomad_vassal
							}
							every_owned_planet = {
								save_event_target_as = target_planet
								give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
									PLANET = event_target:target_planet
									REBEL = fromfrom
									OLD_OWNER = event_target:nomad_vassal
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						fromfrom = {
							set_subject_of = {
								who = root.owner
								preset = preset_nomad_tributary
								allow_instant_negotiation = yes
							}
						}
						root = {
							set_owner = fromfrom
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						from = {
							any_subject = {
								has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
							}
						}
					}
					from = {
						random_subject = {
							limit = {
								has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
							}
							save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
							give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
								PLANET = root
								REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
								OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
							}
							nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
						}
					}
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
						fromfrom = { is_country_type = default }
					}
					fromfrom.capital_scope.planet = {
						create_rebels = {
							name = random
							ethos = fromfrom
							authority = fromfrom
							civics = fromfrom
							origin = origin_default
							species = fromfrom.species
							flag = random
							effect = {
								set_country_type = default
								set_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
								establish_communications_no_message = from
								establish_communications_no_message = fromfrom
								if = {
									limit = {
										is_homicidal = yes
									}
									change_government = {
										civics = random
									}
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_necrophage
									}
									set_origin = origin_necrophage
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_void_dweller_1
									}
									set_origin = origin_void_dwellers
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_void_dweller_2
									}
									set_origin = origin_void_machines
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_cave_dweller
									}
									set_origin = origin_subterranean
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_robot_cave_dweller
									}
									set_origin = origin_subterranean_machines
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = {
										root.owner = { has_origin = origin_tree_of_life }
										has_trait = trait_hive_mind
									}
									set_origin = origin_tree_of_life
								}

								if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_machine_unit
										root.owner = { is_individual_machine = no }
										NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
									}
									shift_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
									change_government = {
										authority = auth_machine_intelligence
										civics = random
									}
								}
								else_if = {
									limit = {
										has_trait = trait_hive_mind
										NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
									}
									shift_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
									change_government = {
										authority = auth_hive_mind
										civics = random
									}
								}
								save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
								set_subject_of = {
									who = root.owner
									preset = preset_nomad_tributary
								}
								give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
									PLANET = root
									REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
									OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
								}
								nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = { #If we are taking the planet from some weird non default country we create a regular vassal
					create_country= {
						name = random
						ethos = from
						authority = from
						civics = from
						remove_invalid_civics = yes # drop nomad-only civics that aren't valid for this non-nomad vassal
						origin = origin_liberated
						species = from.species
						flag = random
						effect = {
							set_country_type = default
							set_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
							establish_communications_no_message = from
							establish_communications_no_message = fromfrom
							from = {
								every_relation = {
									establish_communications_no_message = prevprev
									add_intel_report = { #Ensuring that they know we are purging pops
										category = economy
										level = 1
										who = prevprev
									}
								}
							}
							set_policy = {
								policy = robot_pop_policy
								option = robot_pops_outlawed
								cooldown = yes
							}
							add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = opinion_liberated_us who = from }
							copy_techs_from = {
								target = from
							}
							copy_traditions_from = {
								target = from
							}
							save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
							set_subject_of = {
								who = from
								preset = preset_nomad_tributary
							}
							random_agreement = {
								add_loyalty = 100
							}
							give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
								PLANET = root
								REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
								OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
							}
							nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
							refresh_species_rights = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		else = { #If there was no previous owner there will be no vassal
			destroy_colony = yes
		}
	}
}

# Fired whenever a new owner is set for a planet, following a war or through trade
# This = Planet scope
# From = Country scope (new owner)
# FromFrom = Country scope (previous owner, if any)
carrier_event = { # Purge variant
	id = nomads.5
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOR = {
			is_planet_class = pc_ark
			has_carrier_flag = nomad_recently_settled_flag
		}
		from = { # Nomads should *never* have planets
			is_nomadic = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_valid_civic = civic_machine_terminator
					fromfrom = {
						is_machine_empire = no
					}
				}
				has_policy_flag = nomad_total_war_purge
				has_policy_flag = nomad_total_war_displace
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = { # We split the check for attacker war and defender war into two different if's just to make scripting easier.
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager
				NOMAD = From
				NOMAD_SIDE = defender
				ENEMY = FromFrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = attacker
				TARGET_SYSTEM = root.solar_system
				PLANET = root
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager
				NOMAD = From
				NOMAD_SIDE = attacker
				ENEMY = FromFrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = defender
				TARGET_SYSTEM = root.solar_system
				PLANET = root
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exists = fromfrom
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					from = {
						any_subject = {
							has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
						}
					}
				}
				from = {
					random_subject = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
						}
						save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
						give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
							PLANET = root
							REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
							OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
						}
						nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
						refresh_species_rights = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country= {
					name = random
					ethos = from
					authority = from
					civics = from
					remove_invalid_civics = yes # drop nomad-only civics that aren't valid for this non-nomad vassal
					origin = origin_nomadic_purger
					species = from.species
					flag = random
					effect = {
						set_country_type = default
						set_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
						establish_communications_no_message = from
						establish_communications_no_message = fromfrom
						from = {
							every_relation = {
								establish_communications_no_message = prevprev
								add_intel_report = { #Ensuring that they know we are purging pops
									category = economy
									level = 1
									who = prevprev
								}
							}
						}
						set_policy = {
							policy = robot_pop_policy
							option = robot_pops_outlawed
							cooldown = yes
						}
						add_opinion_modifier = { modifier = opinion_liberated_us who = from }
						copy_techs_from = {
							target = from
						}
						copy_traditions_from = {
							target = from
						}
						save_event_target_as = nomad_vassal
						set_subject_of = {
							who = from
							preset = preset_nomadic_purger
						}
						random_agreement = {
							add_loyalty = 100
						}
						give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
							PLANET = root
							REBEL = event_target:nomad_vassal
							OLD_OWNER = fromfrom
						}
						nomad_vassal_join_overlord_wars_effect = yes
						refresh_species_rights = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		else = { #If there was no previous owner there will be no vassal
			destroy_colony = yes
		}
	}
}

# A pop has finished purging
# This = Planet scope
# From = Country
# FromFrom = Pop group
# local_pop_amount = variable of how many pops were purged
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.10
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from? = {
			has_origin = origin_nomadic_purger
		}
		has_current_purge = no
		is_controlled_by = FROM
	}

	immediate = { # We have no more pops to purge, time to abandon this planet
		if = {
			limit = {
				from = { num_owned_planets <= 1 }
			}
			from = {
				set_timed_country_flag = { # We are about to delete this country and we don't want anything odd happening
					flag = supress_country_destroyed_message
					days = 2
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = minerals
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = food
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = energy
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = alloys
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = consumer_goods
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = trade
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = volatile_motes
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = exotic_gases
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = rare_crystals
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = sr_living_metal
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = sr_zro
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = sr_dark_matter
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = nanites
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = minor_artifacts
					TARGET = overlord
				}
				transfer_resource_to_empire = {
					RESOURCE = astral_threads
					TARGET = overlord
				}
			}
		}
		destroy_colony = yes
	}
}

# From = system
# FromFrom = country (previous owner)
# This = country (new owner)
country_event = {
	id = nomads.15
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = { # We split the check for attacker war and defender war into two different if's just to make scripting easier.
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager_no_planet
				NOMAD = Root
				NOMAD_SIDE = attacker
				ENEMY = FromFrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = defender
				TARGET_SYSTEM = from
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager_no_planet
				NOMAD = Root
				NOMAD_SIDE = defender
				ENEMY = FromFrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = attacker
				TARGET_SYSTEM = from
			}
		}
		else_if = { #If we are the Khan we give the system to our system holder
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = heir_of_the_khan_khan
				exists = event_target:marauder_country_1
			}
			event_target:marauder_country_1 = {
				from.starbase = {
					set_owner = prev
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { #If we have a vassal we give the system to them
			limit = {
				exists = fromfrom
				any_subject = {
					has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
				}
			}
			random_subject = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = nomad_vassal@fromfrom
				}
				from.starbase = {
					set_owner = prev
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { #If we have no vassal we give the system to the closest ally
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager_no_claim
				NOMAD = Root
				NOMAD_SIDE = attacker
				ENEMY = FromFrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = defender
				TARGET_SYSTEM = from
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			inline_script = {
				script = events/nomad_total_war_ally_system_manager_no_claim
				NOMAD = Root
				NOMAD_SIDE = defender
				ENEMY = FromFrom
				ENEMY_SIDE = attacker
				TARGET_SYSTEM = from
			}
		}
		else = { #No vassal, no allies, no fleets.
			from.starbase = {
				fleet = { destroy_fleet = this }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fired by: on_game_start_country
# Starts the Operational Reserves situation and Star Journal chain (Star Seekers only).
# Also relocates all starting fleets to orbit a random non-star planet in their system.
country_event = {
	id = nomads.20
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		start_situation = {
			type = situation_nomad_economy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_star_seeker_empire = yes
			}
			begin_event_chain = {
				event_chain = nomad_star_journal_chain
				target = this
			}
			add_event_chain_counter = {
				event_chain = nomad_star_journal_chain
				counter = star_journal_progress
				amount = 1
			}
			enable_mission = {
				name = NOMAD_STAR_JOURNAL_UNKNOWN_SIGHTS
			}
		}
		every_owned_fleet = {
			move_nomadic_fleet_to_random_system_planet_effect = yes
		}
		# Remove the dummy binary broken pair anchor in Black Hole systems.
		# Nomads have no borders, so random_planet_within_border cannot be used here.
		if = {
			limit = { exists = capital_scope }
			capital_scope.solar_system = {
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						has_carrier_flag = delete_me_planet
					}
					remove_planet = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

ship_event = {
	id = nomads.30
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			is_star_seeker_empire = yes
		}
		from = {
			NOT = {
				has_star_flag = nomad_visited_system@fromfrom
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner? = {
			change_variable = {
				which = visited_systems_nomad
				value = 1
			}
			add_event_chain_counter = {
				event_chain = nomad_star_journal_chain
				counter = star_journal_progress
				amount = 1
			}
		}
		from = {
			set_timed_star_flag = {
				flag = nomad_visited_system@fromfrom
				days = 3600
			}
		}
		ship_event = {
			id = nomads.31
		}
		ship_event = {
			id = nomads.32
		}
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

							value = 1

					owner? = {

							which = visited_systems_nomad

					}

				}

# Nomad fleet leaves a system owned by a country with closed borders
# Sets a timed flag so cb_expel_nomads stays valid while the fleet is jumping between systems
# Scope = Fleet
# From = System
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.35
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
		}
		from? = {
			space_owner? = {
				NOT = { is_same_value = root.owner }
				is_country_type = default
				has_closed_borders = root.owner
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			space_owner = {
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = nomad_trespassing@root.owner
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

ship_event = {
	id = nomads.36
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			is_star_seeker_empire = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner? = {
					check_variable = {
						which = visited_systems_nomad
						value >= 50
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				random_situation = {
					limit = {
						is_situation_type = situation_nomad_economy
					}
					set_situation_approach = situation_nomad_economy_harvest_everything
					# Snapshot reserves so the Festival upkeep drains them evenly over its duration.
					export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
						trigger = situation_progress
						variable = celebration_reserves_at_start
						rounded = yes
					}
					set_variable = {
						which = celebration_months_remaining
						value = @celebration_duration_months_6
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = celebration_active
				set_variable = {
					which = visited_systems_nomad
					value = 1
				}
				reset_event_chain_counter = {
					event_chain = nomad_star_journal_chain
					counter = star_journal_progress
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = nomads.37
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
		is_star_seeker_empire = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		# Switching to Conserve ends any active Festival directly (cooldown + cleanup),
		# rather than relying on on_arkship_mobile firing from a scripted un-encamp.
		end_nomad_festival_effect = yes
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				is_system_locked = yes
			}
			set_system_locked = no
		}
	}
}

# Festival duration countdown, fired monthly by situation_nomad_economy's on_monthly
# This = situation
situation_event = {
	id = nomads.38
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		current_situation_approach = situation_nomad_economy_harvest_everything
	}

	immediate = {
		# Back-fill tracking for Festivals already running before this change (legacy saves).
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { NOT = { has_country_flag = celebration_active } }
			}
			owner = { set_country_flag = celebration_active }
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = situation_progress
				variable = celebration_reserves_at_start
				rounded = yes
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = celebration_months_remaining
				value = @celebration_duration_months_6
			}
		}
		# Count the Festival down; it ends after @celebration_duration_months_6 months.
		change_variable = {
			which = celebration_months_remaining
			value = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = celebration_months_remaining
					value <= 0
				}
			}
			owner = {
				end_nomad_festival_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

# Nomad excavates owned dig site WITHOUT permission
# This = Fleet ( science vessel )
# From = Archaeological Site
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.40
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = solar_system.owner
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_tradition = tr_archivism_frontier_archaeology
			NOT = { has_research_agreement = root.solar_system.owner }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		# Upset the solar system owner
		solar_system.owner = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_arkship_archeological_theft
				who = root.owner
			}
		}
		#message owner
		solar_system.owner  = {
			create_message = {
				type = MESSAGE_ARCHAEOLOGY_STAGE_FINISHED_NOMAD_NO_PERMISSION_OWNER
				localization = MESSAGE_ARCHAEOLOGY_STAGE_FINISHED_NOMAD_NO_PERMISSION_OWNER_DESC
				days = 30
				target = root
			}
		}
		#message nomad
		create_message = {
			type = MESSAGE_ARCHAEOLOGY_STAGE_FINISHED_NOMAD_NO_PERMISSION_OWNER
			localization = MESSAGE_ARCHAEOLOGY_STAGE_FINISHED_NOMAD_NO_PERMISSION_DESC
			days = 30
			target = this
		}
	}
}

# Nomad excavates owned dig site WITH permission
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.41
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = solar_system.owner
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_research_agreement = root.solar_system.owner
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		#grant a reward to the solar system owner
		solar_system.owner = {
			random_list = { #grant monthly research
				1 = {
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = physics_research
								value = @tier2researchreward
								min = @tier2researchmin
								max = @tier2researchmax
							}
						}
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = society_research
								value = @tier2researchreward
								min = @tier2researchmin
								max = @tier2researchmax
							}
						}
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = engineering_research
								value = @tier2researchreward
								min = @tier2researchmin
								max = @tier2researchmax
							}
						}
					}
				}
				3 = {
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = physics_research
								value = @tier3researchreward
								min = @tier3researchmin
								max = @tier3researchmax
							}
						}
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = society_research
								value = @tier3researchreward
								min = @tier3researchmin
								max = @tier3researchmax
							}
						}
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = engineering_research
								value = @tier3researchreward
								min = @tier3researchmin
								max = @tier3researchmax
							}
						}
					}
				}
				1 = {
					random_list = {
						1 = {
							add_monthly_resource_mult = {
								resource = physics_research
								value = @tier4researchreward
								min = @tier4researchmin
								max = @tier4researchmax
							}
						}

								value = @tier4researchreward
								min = @tier4researchmin
								max = @tier4researchmax
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = { #grant artifacts
				5 = { small_artifact_reward = yes }
				3 = { medium_artifact_reward = yes }
				1 = { large_artifact_reward = yes }
			}
		}
		#message owner
		solar_system.owner  = {
			create_message = {
				type = MESSAGE_ARCHAEOLOGY_STAGE_FINISHED_NOMAD_PERMISSION
				localization = MESSAGE_ARCHAEOLOGY_STAGE_FINISHED_NOMAD_PERMISSION_DESC
				days = 30
				target = root
			}
		}

}

#######################
# Arkship Readiness Checklist
#######################

# Initialise checklist.
country_event = {
	id = nomads.50
	title = nomads.50.name
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = nomads.50.default.desc
			success_text = {
				text = nomads.50.shields
				has_country_flag = checklist_shield_realignment
			}
			success_text = {
				text = nomads.50.comms
				has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
			}
			success_text = {
				text = nomads.50.sensors
				has_country_flag = checklist_sensors_calibration
			}
			success_text = {
				text = nomads.50.coolant
				has_country_flag = checklist_flush_coolant
			}
			success_text = {
				text = nomads.50.hangars
				has_country_flag = checklist_cluttered_hangars
			}
			success_text = {
				text = nomads.50.harvest
				has_country_flag = checklist_harvest_resources
			}
			text = nomads.50.end.desc
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_arkship_in_orbit
	show_sound = event_ambient_arkship_engine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	auto_opens = no
	notification_event_icon = "GFX_message_arkship_malfunction"
	notification_event_icon_frame = 2
	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
		is_ai = no
	}

	immediate = {
		begin_event_chain = {
			event_chain = "nomad_checklist_chain"
			target = capital_scope.ship
		}
		begin_checklist_harvest_resources_effect = yes
		while = {
			count = 2
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					# Shield Calibration
					begin_checklist_shield_realignment_effect = yes
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = checklist_shield_realignment
					}
				}
				1 = {
					# Update Comms Frequencies
					begin_checklist_decipher_signal_effect = yes
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
					}
				}
				1 = {
					# Recalibrate Sensors
					begin_checklist_sensor_calibration_effect = yes
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = checklist_sensors_calibration
					}
				}
				1 = {
					# Flush Coolant
					begin_checklist_flush_coolant_effect = yes
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = checklist_flush_coolant
					}
				}
				1 = {
					# Cluttered Hangar Bays
					begin_checklist_clear_hangar_bays_effect = yes
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = checklist_cluttered_hangars
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ACKNOWLEDGED
		tooltip = {
			begin_event_chain = {
				event_chain = "nomad_checklist_chain"
				target = capital_scope.ship
			}
		}
	}
}

# Complete NOMAD_CHECKLIST_SHIELD_REALIGNMENT
# Fired by on_damage_taken
# This = damaged ship
# From = attacker ship
ship_event = {
	id = nomads.51
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_country_flag = checklist_shield_realignment
		}
		colony? = {
			has_modifier = checklist_unaligned_shields
		}
		check_modifier_value = { modifier = ship_shield_reduction value = 0 }
		has_shield_percentage < 0.1
	}

	immediate = {
		owner? = {
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission =  NOMAD_CHECKLIST_SHIELD_REALIGNMENT
				counter = SHIELD_REALIGNMENT
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Increment "Unique Stars Surveyed" counter for NOMAD_CHECKLIST_SENSOR_CALIBRATION

	hide_window = yes

# Source of strange signal has been surveyed.
# Fired by on_system_survey_ship
# Scope = ship
# From = system
ship_event = {
	id = nomads.53
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
		}
		from.owner? = {
			is_same_value = event_target:comms_signal_system@owner
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner? = {
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission =  NOMAD_CHECKLIST_DECIPHER_SIGNAL
				counter = SIGNAL_DECIPHERED
				amount = 1
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = event_target:comms_signal_system@from.owner
	}
}

# Source of strange signal has been deciphered.
# Fired by on_first_contact_finished
# This = first contact scope
# From = other country
first_contact_event = {
	id = nomads.54
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				from = {
					is_nomadic = yes
					has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
				}
				owner = {
					is_same_value = event_target:comms_source@from
				}
			}
			AND = {
				owner = {
					is_nomadic = yes
					has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
				}
				from = {
					is_same_value = event_target:comms_source@root.owner
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				from = {
					is_nomadic = yes
					has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
				}
				owner = {
					is_same_value = event_target:comms_source@from
				}
			}
			from = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission =  NOMAD_CHECKLIST_DECIPHER_SIGNAL
					counter = SIGNAL_DECIPHERED
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_nomadic = yes
					has_country_flag = checklist_decipher_signal
				}
				from = {
					is_same_value = event_target:comms_source@root.owner
				}
			}
			owner = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission =  NOMAD_CHECKLIST_DECIPHER_SIGNAL
					counter = SIGNAL_DECIPHERED
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

####################
# AI Helper Events #
####################

country_event = {
	id = nomads.80
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		is_nomadic = yes
		last_increased_tech = tech_arkship_construction
	}

	immediate = {
		capital_scope = {
			solar_system = {
				save_event_target_as = target_system
			}
			ship = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_civilian_arkship = yes }
					create_arkship_effect = {
						TYPE = civilian_arkship
						OWNER = root
						LOCATION = event_target:target_system
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_science_arkship = yes }
					create_arkship_effect = {
						TYPE = science_arkship
						OWNER = root
						LOCATION = event_target:target_system
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { is_military_arkship = yes }
					create_arkship_effect = {
						TYPE = military_arkship
						OWNER = root
						LOCATION = event_target:target_system
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Re-enable disabled arkships after a war ends
# ROOT = Loser, FROM = Main Winner
country_event = {
	id = nomads.94
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			from = { is_nomadic = yes }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		# Re-enable the loser's disabled arkships
		every_owned_fleet = {
			limit = { is_arkship_fleet = yes }
			every_owned_ship = {
				limit = {
					is_arkship_ship = yes
					is_disabled = yes
				}
				repair_amount = 1000
				set_disabled = no
				remove_ship_flag = disabled_by_default_empire_event
			}
		}
		# Re-enable the loser's disabled waystations
		every_owned_fleet = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_ship = { is_waystation_ship = yes  is_disabled = yes }
			}
			every_owned_ship = {
				limit = { is_waystation_ship = yes  is_disabled = yes }
				repair_amount = 1000
				set_disabled = no
			}
		}
		# Re-enable the winner's disabled arkships and waystations
		from = {
			every_owned_fleet = {
				limit = { is_arkship_fleet = yes }
				every_owned_ship = {
					limit = {
						is_arkship_ship = yes
						is_disabled = yes
					}
					repair_amount = 1000
					set_disabled = no
					remove_ship_flag = disabled_by_default_empire_event
				}
			}
			every_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_ship = { is_waystation_ship = yes  is_disabled = yes }
				}
				every_owned_ship = {
					limit = { is_waystation_ship = yes  is_disabled = yes }
					repair_amount = 1000
					set_disabled = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

## Place pops on newly built Arkships
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.95
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		carrier_is_type = ship
		is_capital = no
	}

	immediate = {
		while = {
			count = 10
			create_pop_group = {
				species = owner_main_species
			}
		}
	}
}

#Notify about losing a waystation
# THIS = Starbase (Not The Ship)
# FROM = Previous Owner Country
starbase_event = {
	id = nomads.99
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_waystation_starbase = yes
		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		create_message = {
			recipient = FROM
			type = MESSAGE_WAYSTATION_LOST
			localization = MESSAGE_WAYSTATION_LOST_DESC
			target = solar_system
			days = @toast_important_message_days
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = WAYSTATION
				scope = THIS
			}
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = SYSTEM
				scope = solar_system
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = nomads.100
	title = "nomads.100.name"
	desc = {
		text = "nomads.100a.desc"
		text = "nomads.100b.desc"
		text = "nomads.100c.desc"
	}
	# desc_clear = yes
	# option_clear = yes
	event_message_type = ENCLAVE_DIPLOMACY
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = enclave_champions_forge_window
	custom_gui_option = enclave_champions_forge_option
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country
		room = champions_forge_room
	}
	location = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_fleet

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country
		NOT = {	has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_ignores }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_encountered
	}

	# Standard options
	inline_script = enclaves/champions_forge_guardians_options
}

# Champions Forge Enclave Ignore Diplomacy (after stealing from you or being attacked by you)
# via on_custom_diplomacy | from = Champions Forge Enclave country

	id = nomads.105
	title = "nomads.105.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_encountered
		}
		text = "nomads.105.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_encountered }
		}
		text = "nomads.105.desc.unknown"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_space_station
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter
	location = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_fleet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	event_message_type = ENCLAVE_DIPLOMACY

	trigger = {
		from = {
			is_country_type = enclave
			has_country_flag = champions_forge_enclave_country
		}
		has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_ignores
	}

	option = {
		name = {
			exclusive_trigger = { has_valid_civic = civic_fanatic_purifiers }
			text = "SCUM"
		}
		name = {
			exclusive_trigger = { has_valid_civic = civic_hive_devouring_swarm }
			text = "TASTY"
		}
		name = {
			exclusive_trigger = { has_valid_civic = civic_machine_terminator }
			text = "EXTERMINATE"
		}
		# Previously met the Champions Forge Enclave
		name = {
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_encountered
			}
			text = "nomads.105.a"
		}
		# Not met the Champions Forge Enclave yet
		name = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_encountered
				}
			}
			text = "PECULIAR"
		}
	}
}

# Champions Forge Introduce a Paragon
country_event = {
	id = nomads.120
	base = nomads.100
	desc_clear = yes
	option_clear = yes
	desc = "nomads.120.desc"
	event_message_type = ENCLAVE_DIPLOMACY


	#Back to menu
	option = {
		name = enclave.410.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nomads.100 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nomads.120.a
		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = nomadic_paragon_cooldown_tt
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nomadic_paragon_cooldown
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = nomadic_paragon_already_hired
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_revenant
					has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_sage
					has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_naturalist
					has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_caregiver
					has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_champion
					has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_princess
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = nomadic_paragon_all_hired
				NAND = {
					can_hire_nomadic_paragon_1 = no
					can_hire_nomadic_paragon_2 = no
					can_hire_nomadic_paragon_3 = no
					can_hire_nomadic_paragon_4 = no
					can_hire_nomadic_paragon_5 = no
					can_hire_nomadic_paragon_6 = no
				}
			}
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = energy
				value >= 10
				mult = root.trigger:empire_size
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			energy = -10
			mult = root.trigger:empire_size
		}
		custom_tooltip = nomadic_paragon_explanation
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = {
				flag = nomadic_paragon_cooldown
				days = 3600
			}
			set_saved_date = {
				key = nomadic_paragon_timer
				days_from_present = 3600
				expires = 3600
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1500
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = GOODBYE
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

# Champions Forge Combat Briefing Renewal Reminder
# Scheduled 10 years after a cfl_combat_data purchase
country_event = {
	id = nomads.125
	title = "nomads.125.name"
	desc = "nomads.125.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_champions_forge
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter
	location = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_fleet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	event_message_type = ENCLAVE_DIPLOMACY

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country
		is_diplomatic = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_ignores }
		NOT = { has_modifier = cfl_combat_data }
		num_rivals > 0
	}

	# Renew the briefing
	option = {
		name = "nomads.125.a"
		inline_script = {
			script = events/resource_cost_with_allow
			RESOURCE = trade
			AMOUNT = 2500
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = cfl_combat_data
			days = 3600
		}
		custom_tooltip = opinion10
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country = {
				add_trust = {
					who = root
					amount = 10
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.125
				days = 3600
			}
		}
	}

	# Decline
	option = {
		name = "nomads.125.b"
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

# ESTABLISH COMMUNICATIONS

# Champions Forge gatekeeper event
# via on_custom_diplomacy | this = target country (player); from = country being contacted
country_event = {
	id = nomads.150
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_champions_forge_event = no
		from = {
			has_country_flag = champions_forge_enclave_country
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { exists = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country }
			}
			from = {
				save_global_event_target_as = champions_forge_enclave_country
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = nomads.100 }
	}
}

# Communications established (establishing scopes)
# via finish_first_contact_effect / action.11 / leviathans.98
# this = enclave country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.155
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# The 'ignores' flag may be set (indefinitely) during an act of aggression towards the Champions Forge Enclave, OR as a timed flag following certain actions the Champions Forge Enclave takes towards the player.
	immediate = {
		from = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = enclave_champions_forge_ignores }
				country_event = { id = nomads.105 } # Champions Forge refuse comms.
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = nomads.160 } # Champions Forge introduction
			}
		}
	}
}

# Champions Forge invitation to tournament
country_event = {
	id = nomads.250
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = champions_forge_tournament_ongoing
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		event_target:champions_forge_enclave_fleet.solar_system = {
			save_global_event_target_as = champions_forge_enclave_system
		}
		set_country_flag = champions_forge_tournament_ongoing
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_heavy_late }
			remove_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_heavy_late
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_late }
			remove_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_late
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_mid }
			remove_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_mid
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_mid }
			remove_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_mid
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_early }
			remove_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_early
		}
		change_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value = 1 }
		random_list = {
			1 = { # Fleet Size 500
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value >= 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value <= 3 }
				}
				set_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_heavy_late
			}
			1 = { # Fleet Size 200
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value = 4 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value <= 2 }
				}
				set_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_late
			}
			1 = { # Fleet Size 100
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value >= 5 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value = 3 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value = 1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_mid
			}
			1 = { # Fleet Size 50
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value >= 4 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value = 2 }
				}
				set_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_mid
			}
			1 = { # Fleet Size 25
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value >= 3 }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					check_variable = { which = cfl_tournament_count value = 1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_early
			}
		}
		every_relation = {
			limit = {
				is_country_type = default
				has_communications = prev
				is_ai = no
				is_diplomatic = yes
				is_homicidal = no
				is_level_4_player_crisis = no
				NOR = {
					has_country_flag = champions_forge_stop_invitations
					has_event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
				}
			}
			event_target:champions_forge_enclave_system = {
				set_surveyed = {
					surveyed = yes
					surveyor = prev
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.255
				days = 1 # Delay one day to let the previous system survey occur
			}
		}

		event_target:champions_forge_enclave_system = {
			system_event = {
				id = nomads.260
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hey Country, do you want to join the tournament?
country_event = {
	id = nomads.255
	title = "nomads.255.name"
	desc = {
		text = "nomads.255.desc"
		trigger = { NOT = { has_relic = r_cfl_trophy } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = "nomads.255.desc.relic"
		trigger = { has_relic = r_cfl_trophy }
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_champions_forge
	show_sound = event_public_unrest
	event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
	location = capital_scope.solar_system
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		begin_event_chain = {
			event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
			target = this
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "nomads.255.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.255.a.tooltip"
		# Only players get the special project, AI empires are spawned when the first player finishes the project
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "CHAMPIONS_FORGE_TRAVEL"
			location = capital_scope.solar_system.star
			owner = ROOT
		}
		set_country_flag = champions_forge_interest
		remove_country_flag = champions_forge_stop_invitations
		set_country_flag = champions_forge_send_invitations
	}
	option = {
		name = "nomads.255.b"
		end_event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
	}
	option = {
		name = "nomads.255.c"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.255.c.tooltip"
		remove_country_flag = champions_forge_send_invitations
		set_country_flag = champions_forge_stop_invitations
		end_event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_relic = r_cfl_trophy
			}
			remove_relic = r_cfl_trophy
		}
	}
}

# Champions Forge start tournament
system_event = {
	id = nomads.260
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from = {
			set_country_flag = champions_forge_battle_started
			every_relation = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					is_country_type = default
					is_diplomatic = yes
				}
				if = { # We want a minimum of contestants of either the amount of countires the Enclave knows or 12
					limit = {
						root = {
							count_fleet_in_system = {
								count < 12
								limit = {
									controller = {
										is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
									}
									is_disabled = no
								}
							}
						}
					}
					event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country = {
    					switch = {
     						trigger = has_country_flag
        						champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_heavy_late 	= {
            						prev = {
            							create_ai_champions_forge_contestant = 	{ FLEET_SIZE = 500 }
            						}
        						}
        						champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_late 	= {
            						prev = {
        						        create_ai_champions_forge_contestant = 	{ FLEET_SIZE = 200 }
        						    }
        						}
        						champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_medium_mid 	= {
        						    prev = {
        						        create_ai_champions_forge_contestant = 	{ FLEET_SIZE = 100 }
        						    }
        						}
								champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_mid = 	{
        						    prev = {
        						        create_ai_champions_forge_contestant = 	{ FLEET_SIZE = 50 }
        						    }
        						}
								champions_of_the_forge_weight_class_small_early 	= {
        						    prev = {
        						        create_ai_champions_forge_contestant = 	{ FLEET_SIZE = 25 }
        						    }
        						}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				count_fleet_in_system = {
					count >= 2
					limit = {
						controller = {
							is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
						}
						is_disabled = no
					}
				}
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = champions_forge_contestant_country
				}
				remove_country_flag = champions_forge_contestant_country
				country_event = {
					id = nomads.270
				}
			}

			every_fleet_in_system = {
				limit = {
					has_fleet_flag = champions_forge_contestant_fleet
				}
				clear_orders = yes
				set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
				set_aggro_range = 1000
				set_fleet_stance = aggressive
			}

			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
				}
				country_event = {
					id = nomads.265
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_fleet_in_system = {
					count <= 1
					limit = {
						controller = {
							is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
						}
						is_disabled = no
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
				}
				country_event = {
					id = nomads.266
				}
			}
			# Not enough participants, return to flying around the galaxy
			event_target:champions_forge_enclave_fleet = {
				set_timed_fleet_flag = {
					flag = champions_forge_match_cooldown
					years = 20
				}
				champions_forge_departure_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Champions Forge set every champion country hostile to each other
country_event = {
	id = nomads.265
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
			}
			set_faction_hostility = {
				target = root
				set_hostile = yes
				set_neutral = no
				set_friendly = no
			}
			set_hostile = root
		}
	}
}

# If any fleets are here we tell the owners that the fight isn't happening
country_event = {
	id = nomads.266
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		overlord? = {
			create_message = {
				type = CFL_NO_TOURNAMENT
				localization = CFL_NO_TOURNAMENT_DESC
				days = 30
			}
		}
		every_controlled_fleet = {
			limit = {
				has_fleet_flag = player_champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			}
			remove_fleet_flag = champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			remove_fleet_flag = player_champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			owner = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_leader = {
							has_leader_flag = temp_contestant_admiral
						}
					}
					random_owned_leader = {
						limit = { has_leader_flag = temp_contestant_admiral }
						kill_leader = { show_notification = no }
					}
				}
			}
			end_fleet_contract = {
				initiator = this.controller
				reason = cancelled
			}
			every_owned_ship = {
				set_disable_at_health = no
			}
			clear_orders = yes
			set_mia = mia_return_home
			set_mia_return_delay = 180
		}
		every_controlled_fleet = {
			limit = {
				has_fleet_flag = champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			}
			destroy_fleet = this
		}
	}
}

	id = nomads.270
	title = "nomads.270.name"
	desc = "nomads.270.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_champions_forge
	show_sound = event_public_unrest
	location = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_system
	event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
	}

# Put a flag on the third, second, and first place teams.
# Fired by: on_space_battle_over
# This = owner of fleet 1 (winner)
# From = owner of fleet 2 (loser)
# FromFrom = fleet 1
# FromFromFrom = fleet 2
country_event = {
	id = nomads.275
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
	}

	immediate = {
		# from = losing country
		from = {
			# fromfrom = winning fleet
			from = {
				# fromfromfrom = losing fleet
				from = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							solar_system = {
								count_fleet_in_system = {
									count = 2
									limit = {
										controller = {
											is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
										}
										is_disabled = no
									}
								}
							}
						}
						set_fleet_flag = champions_forge_third_place
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							solar_system = {
								count_fleet_in_system = {
									count = 1
									limit = {
										controller = {
											is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
										}
										is_disabled = no
									}
								}
							}
						}
						set_fleet_flag = champions_forge_second_place
						prev = {
							set_fleet_flag = champions_forge_first_place
						}
						solar_system = {
							system_event = {
								id = nomads.280
								days = 30
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Notify the winning countries, return the fleets to their owners, and destroy the team countries
system_event = {
	id = nomads.280
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Notify winners and losers
		every_fleet_in_system = {
			controller = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_subject = yes }
					save_event_target_as = cfl_wrapper
					random_playable_country = {
						limit = {
							event_target:cfl_wrapper = {
								has_relation_flag = {
									who = prev
									flag = cfl_parent_empire
								}
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = cfl_contestant_parent
					}
				}
			}
			switch = {
				trigger = has_fleet_flag
				champions_forge_third_place = {
					remove_fleet_flag = champions_forge_third_place
					event_target:cfl_contestant_parent = {
						country_event = { id = nomads.285 }
					}
				}
				champions_forge_second_place = {
					remove_fleet_flag = champions_forge_second_place
					event_target:cfl_contestant_parent = {
						country_event = { id = nomads.290 }
					}
				}
				champions_forge_first_place = {
					remove_fleet_flag = champions_forge_first_place
					event_target:cfl_contestant_parent = {
						country_event = { id = nomads.295 }
					}
				}
				default = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_fleet_flag = champions_forge_contestant_fleet
						}
						event_target:cfl_contestant_parent = {
							country_event = { id = nomads.305 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		# Enable all fleets
		every_ship_in_system = {
			limit = {
				is_disabled = yes
			}
			set_disabled = no
		}

		# Return the fleets to their owners
		every_fleet_in_system = {
			limit = {
				has_fleet_flag = player_champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			}
			remove_fleet_flag = champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			remove_fleet_flag = player_champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			owner = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_leader = {
							has_leader_flag = temp_contestant_admiral
						}
					}
					random_owned_leader = {
						limit = { has_leader_flag = temp_contestant_admiral }
						kill_leader = { show_notification = no }
					}
				}
			}
			end_fleet_contract = {
				initiator = this.controller
				reason = cancelled
			}
			every_owned_ship = {
				set_disable_at_health = no
			}
			clear_orders = yes
			set_mia = mia_return_home
			set_mia_return_delay = 180
		}
		every_fleet_in_system = {
			limit = {
				has_fleet_flag = champions_forge_contestant_fleet
			}
			destroy_fleet = this
		}
		# Destroy the team countries
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_country_type = champions_forge_contestant
			}
			destroy_country = yes
		}
		# Remove the flag for ongoing Champions Forge tournaments
		event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country = {
			remove_country_flag = champions_forge_tournament_ongoing
			remove_country_flag = champions_forge_battle_started
		}

		# Return to flying around the galaxy
		event_target:champions_forge_enclave_fleet = {
			set_timed_fleet_flag = {
				flag = champions_forge_match_cooldown
				years = 20
			}
			champions_forge_departure_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# First place notification
country_event = {
	id = nomads.295
	title = "nomads.295.name"
	desc = "nomads.295.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_champions_forge
	show_sound = event_public_unrest
	location = event_target:champions_forge_enclave_system
	event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nomads.295.a
		add_resource = { trade = 5000 }
		if = { #This should never happen
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_relic = r_cfl_trophy }
			}
			add_relic = r_cfl_trophy
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			inverted_switch = {
				trigger = has_global_flag
				cfl_winner_1_set = {
					random_list = {
						1 = { #25% of the time a Fallen Empire has already won this once
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								count_country = {
									count =  0
									limit = {
										is_fallen_empire = yes
									}
								}
							}
							random_country = {
								limit = {
									is_fallen_empire = yes
								}
								save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_1
							}
							save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_2
							set_global_flag = cfl_winner_1_set
							set_global_flag = cfl_winner_2_set
						}
						3 = { # Most of the time they have not won
							save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_1
							set_global_flag = cfl_winner_1_set
						}
					}
				}
				cfl_winner_2_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_2
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_2_set
				}
				cfl_winner_3_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_3
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_3_set
				}
				cfl_winner_4_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_4
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_4_set
				}
				cfl_winner_5_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_5
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_5_set
				}
				cfl_winner_6_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_6
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_6_set
				}
				cfl_winner_7_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_7
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_7_set
				}
				cfl_winner_8_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_8
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_8_set
				}
				cfl_winner_9_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_9
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_9_set
				}
				cfl_winner_10_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_10
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_10_set
				}
				cfl_winner_11_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_11
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_11_set
				}
				cfl_winner_12_set = {
					save_global_event_target_as = cfl_winner_12
					set_global_flag = cfl_winner_12_set
				}
				default = {}
			}
		}
		end_event_chain = champions_forge_tournament_chain
		custom_tooltip = opinion30
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:champions_forge_enclave_country = {
				add_trust = {
					who = root
					amount = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# CHAMPIONS FORGE LIVE! DESTROYED

# This = owner of ship 1 (destroyed)
# From = owner of ship 2 (combatant)
# FromFrom = ship 1
# FromFromFrom = ship 2 # can be invalid if damage is done via other methods (like scripted action)
country_event = {
	id = nomads.400
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_country_type = enclave
		has_country_flag = champions_forge_enclave_country
		FROMFROM = {
			is_ship_size = military_arkship_champions_forge
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		FROMFROM = {
			solar_system = { save_event_target_as = champions_forge_destruction_system }
		}
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = champions_forge_destroyer
			country_event = { id = nomads.405 }
			save_event_target_as = champions_forge_destroyer
		}
		every_playable_country = {
			limit = {
				has_communications = ROOT
				NOT = { is_country = event_target:champions_forge_destroyer }
			}
			country_event = { id = nomads.410 }
		}
		random_playable_country = {
			observer_event = { id = observer.105 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

##### Heirs of the Khan #####

country_event = {
	id = nomads.500
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
		NOT = { has_country_flag = won_khan_duel }
		exists = event_target:marauder_heir
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			16 = { #We did not spawn hunters today
				country_event = { id = nomads.500 days = 200 random = 100 }
			}
			5 = { #Spawning hunters
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					capital_scope = { has_carrier_flag = nomad_recent_combat }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					capital_scope = { has_carrier_flag = nomad_recent_encamped }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					capital_scope = { has_carrier_flag = nomad_recent_accepted_contract }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					capital_scope = { has_carrier_flag = nomad_recent_war }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					root.owner = {
						has_country_flag = intimidated_marauder_hunters
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = nomads.505 }
			}
			3 = { #Spawn Contract
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					check_variable = {
						which = defeated_heirs_hunters_spawner
						value = 0
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					any_issued_mission = {
						OR = {
							is_mission_type = contract_intercept_raid_heirs
							is_mission_type = contract_destroy_station_heirs
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					root.owner = {
						has_country_flag = intimidated_marauder_hunters
					}
				}
				random_system = {
					limit = {
						distance = {
							source = root.capital_scope.solar_system
							min_jumps = 1
							max_jumps = 5
						}
						NOR = {
							has_star_flag = hostile_system
							has_star_flag = guardian
							has_star_flag = marauder_system
							has_star_flag = lcluster1
							has_star_flag = lcluster2
							has_star_flag = lcluster3
							has_star_flag = lcluster4
							has_star_flag = lcluster5
							has_star_flag = lcluster_lgate
							is_fe_cluster = yes
						}
						root = {
							intel_level = {
								level > none
								system = prev
							}
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = contract_system
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = contract_intercept_raid_heirs_issued
						}
						root = {
							issue_contract = {
								contract = contract_intercept_raid_heirs
								location = event_target:contract_system
								target = root
							}
							set_timed_country_flag = {
								flag = contract_intercept_raid_heirs_issued
								days = 2000 # Avoiding getting the same one twice
							}
						}
					}
					1 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = contract_destroy_station_heirs_issued
						}
						root = {
							issue_contract = {
								contract = contract_destroy_station_heirs
								location = event_target:contract_system
								target = root
							}
							set_timed_country_flag = {
								flag = contract_destroy_station_heirs_issued
								days = 2000 # Avoiding getting the same one twice
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					source = root.capital_star
					use_bypasses = no

					min_jumps = 1
					max_jumps = 5
				}
				NOR = {
					has_star_flag = hostile_system
					has_star_flag = guardian
					has_star_flag = marauder_system
					has_star_flag = lcluster1
					has_star_flag = lcluster2
					has_star_flag = lcluster3
					has_star_flag = lcluster4
					has_star_flag = lcluster5
					has_star_flag = lcluster_lgate
					is_fe_cluster = yes
				}
				root = {
					intel_level = {
						level > none
						system = prev
					}
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = contract_system
		}
		issue_contract = {

			location = event_target:contract_system

		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = nomads.505
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { #Clean up the old fleet if it's still around
				exists = event_target:hunter_fleet
				event_target:hunter_fleet = {
					is_in_combat = no
				}
			}
			event_target:hunter_fleet = {
				delete_fleet = this
			}
		}

		capital_scope.ship.fleet = {
			save_event_target_as = hunted_fleet
			set_fleet_flag = hunted_fleet
			solar_system = {
				closest_system = {
					limit = {
						NOR = {
							has_star_flag = guardian
							has_star_flag = hostile_system
						}
					}
					use_bypasses = no
					min_steps = 2
					max_steps = 5
					save_event_target_as = spawning_system
				}
			}

			owner = {
				if = { #Giving the hunters access to more ship designs as the variable increases
					limit = {
						root = {
							check_variable = {
								which = defeated_heirs_hunters
								value < 5
							}
						}
					}
					create_balanced_fleet = {
						name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
						size = root.value:heirs_hunter_fleet_size
						ship_designs = {
							NAME_Outrider
						}
						effect = {
							set_owner = event_target:marauder_heir
							set_location = event_target:spawning_system
							set_fleet_stance = aggressive
							set_fleet_bombardment_stance = indiscriminate
							set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
							set_aggro_range = 150
							set_owner = event_target:marauder_hunters #Real Owner
							save_event_target_as = hunter_fleet
							set_fleet_flag = heirs_hunter_fleet
							set_fleet_settings = {
								spawn_debris = no
							}

							queue_actions = {
								repeat = {
									find_random_fleet = {
										trigger = {
											id = "heirs_100"
											is_same_value = event_target:hunted_fleet
										}
										found_fleet = {
											move_to = this
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						root = {
							check_variable = {
								which = defeated_heirs_hunters
								value >= 5
							}
							check_variable = {
								which = defeated_heirs_hunters
								value < 10
							}
						}
					}
					create_balanced_fleet = {
						name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
						size = root.value:heirs_hunter_fleet_size
						ship_designs = {
							NAME_Outrider
							NAME_Lancer
						}
						effect = {
							set_owner = event_target:marauder_heir
							set_location = event_target:spawning_system
							set_fleet_stance = aggressive
							set_fleet_bombardment_stance = indiscriminate
							set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
							set_aggro_range = 150
							set_owner = event_target:marauder_hunters #Real Owner
							save_event_target_as = hunter_fleet
							set_fleet_flag = heirs_hunter_fleet
							set_fleet_settings = {
								spawn_debris = no
							}

							queue_actions = {
								repeat = {
									find_random_fleet = {
										trigger = {
											id = "heirs_101"
											is_same_value = event_target:hunted_fleet
										}
										found_fleet = {
											move_to = this
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					create_balanced_fleet = {
						name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
						size = root.value:heirs_hunter_fleet_size
						ship_designs = {
							NAME_Outrider
							NAME_Lancer
							NAME_Void_Champion
						}
						effect = {
							set_owner = event_target:marauder_heir
							set_location = event_target:spawning_system
							set_fleet_stance = aggressive
							set_fleet_bombardment_stance = indiscriminate
							set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
							set_aggro_range = 150
							set_owner = event_target:marauder_hunters #Real Owner
							save_event_target_as = hunter_fleet
							set_fleet_flag = heirs_hunter_fleet
							set_fleet_settings = {
								spawn_debris = no
							}

							queue_actions = {
								repeat = {
									find_random_fleet = {
										trigger = {
											id = "heirs_102"
											is_same_value = event_target:hunted_fleet
										}
										found_fleet = {
											move_to = this
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:hunter_fleet = {
					owner = {
						set_faction_hostility = {
							target = root
							set_hostile = yes
							set_neutral = no
						}
					}
					random_list = {
						10 = { #No special interaction

						}
						5 = { #Negotiate at loss effect
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								root.owner = { # No special interaction if you haven't defeated any yet
									check_variable = {
										which = defeated_heirs_hunters
										value = 0
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								add = root.owner.defeated_heirs_hunters
							}
							every_owned_ship = {
								set_disable_at_health = 0.01
								set_ship_flag = marauder_hunter
							}
							set_fleet_flag = will_surrender_heirs
						}
						5 = { #Negotiation at start effect
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								root.owner = {
									check_variable = {
										which = defeated_heirs_hunters
										value = 0
									}
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								add = root.owner.defeated_heirs_hunters
							}
							root.owner = {
								set_relation_flag = {
									who = prev.owner
									flag = negotiate_on_encounter
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = heirs_seen_first_hunters
			}
			create_message = {
				type = HEIRS_HUNTERS_HAVE_SPAWNED
				localization = HEIRS_HUNTERS_HAVE_SPAWNED_DESC
				days = 30
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = ARKSHIP
					scope = capital_scope
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.506
			}
		}

		country_event = {
			id = nomads.500
			days = 1000
			random = 600
		}
	}
}
