# A fleet has entered a system | See also: on_fleet_auto_move_arrival
# Scope = Fleet
# From = System
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.520
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_arkship_fleet = yes
		owner? = {
			has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
		}
		from = {
			has_star_flag = intercept_raid@root.owner
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = heirs_fleet
		from = {
			remove_star_flag = intercept_raid@root.owner #prevent the event from happening multiple times
		}
		owner = {
			remove_point_of_interest = intercept_raid@root.owner
			create_message = {
				type = HEIRS_RAID_INTERCEPTED
				localization = HEIRS_RAID_INTERCEPTED_DESC
				days = 30
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = SYSTEM
					scope = from
				}
			}
			if = { #Giving the hunters access to more ship designs as the variable increases
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = defeated_heirs_hunters
						value < 5
					}
				}
				create_balanced_fleet = {
					name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
					size = root.owner.value:heirs_hunter_fleet_size_small
					ship_designs = {
						NAME_Outrider
					}
					effect = {
						marauder_heir_contract_effect = yes
						queue_actions = {
							find_random_fleet = {
								trigger = {
									id = "intercepting_raid_fleet_1"
									is_same_value = event_target:heirs_fleet
								}
								found_fleet = {
									move_to = this
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = defeated_heirs_hunters
						value >= 5
					}
					check_variable = {
						which = defeated_heirs_hunters
						value < 10
					}
				}
				create_balanced_fleet = {
					name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
					size = root.owner.value:heirs_hunter_fleet_size_small
					ship_designs = {
						NAME_Outrider
						NAME_Lancer
					}
					effect = {
						marauder_heir_contract_effect = yes
						queue_actions = {
							find_random_fleet = {
								trigger = {
									id = "intercepting_raid_fleet_2"
									is_same_value = event_target:heirs_fleet
								}
								found_fleet = {
									move_to = this
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_balanced_fleet = {
					name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
					size = root.owner.value:heirs_hunter_fleet_size_small
					ship_designs = {
						NAME_Outrider
						NAME_Lancer
						NAME_Void_Champion
					}
					effect = {
						marauder_heir_contract_effect = yes
						queue_actions = {
							find_random_fleet = {
								trigger = {
									id = "intercepting_raid_fleet_3"
									is_same_value = event_target:heirs_fleet
								}
								found_fleet = {
									move_to = this
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# This = owner of fleet 1 (destroyed)
# From = owner of fleet 2 (combatant)
# FromFrom = fleet 1
# FromFromFrom = fleet 2
country_event = {
	id = nomads.525
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = heirs_marauder_hunters
		fromfrom = {
			has_fleet_flag = heirs_raider_fleet
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_relation = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_relation_flag = {
					who = root
					flag = contract_heirs_hunter_raid
				}
			}
			root = {
				remove_relation_flag = {
					who = prev
					flag = contract_heirs_hunter_raid
				}
			}
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_intercept_raid_heirs
				counter = contract_progress_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# This = owner of fleet 1 (destroyed)
# From = owner of fleet 2 (combatant)
# FromFrom = fleet 1
# FromFromFrom = fleet 2
country_event = {
	id = nomads.530
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = heirs_marauder_hunters
		fromfrom = {
			OR = {
				has_fleet_flag = heirs_raider_starbase
				has_fleet_flag = heirs_raider_starbase_start
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_relation = {
			limit = {
				reverse_has_relation_flag = {
					who = root
					flag = contract_heirs_hunter_starbase
				}
			}
			root = {
				remove_relation_flag = {
					who = prev
					flag = contract_heirs_hunter_starbase
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					fromfrom = {
						has_fleet_flag = heirs_raider_starbase
					}
				}
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = contract_destroy_station_heirs
					counter = contract_progress_counter
					amount = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = contract_destroy_station_heirs_start
					counter = contract_progress_counter
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			value = 1
		}

		}
	}

ship_event = {
	id = nomads.550
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_ship_flag = marauder_hunter
		fleet = {
			NOT = {
				any_owned_ship = {
					is_disabled = no
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_fleet_flag = heirs_hunters_surrendered }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				from.owner = {
					has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
				}
			}
			from.owner = { country_event = { id = nomads.555 } }
		}
		else = {
			fleet = {
				delete_fleet = this
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_relation_flag = {
						who = root.owner
						flag = negotiate_on_encounter
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		solar_system = {
			random_fleet_in_system = {
				limit = {
					has_fleet_flag = hunted_fleet
					owner = {
						has_relation_flag = {
							who = root.owner
							flag = negotiate_on_encounter
						}
					}
				}
				save_event_target_as = hunted_fleet
				remove_fleet_flag = hunted_fleet
				owner = {
					country_event = { id = nomads.570 }
					remove_relation_flag = {
						who = root.owner
						flag = negotiate_on_encounter
					}
				}
			}
		}
		clear_fleet_actions = this
	}
}

country_event = {
    id = nomads.600
    title = nomads.600.name
    desc = nomads.600.desc
    picture = GFX_evt_khan_throne_room
    show_sound = relic_activation_khans_throne
    location = event_target:marauder_rally_point
    is_triggered_only = yes

	event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate

    immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = dormant_marauders
						has_country_flag = aspiring_khan
					}
				}
				set_faction_hostility = {
					target = root
					set_hostile = no
					set_neutral = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = no
			}
			begin_event_chain = {
				event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate
				target = root
			}
			create_point_of_interest = {
				id = marauder_rally_point
				name = heirs_khan_rally_point_name
				desc = heirs_khan_rally_point_desc
				event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate
				location = event_target:marauder_rally_point
			}
		}
    }
    option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
        name = nomads.600.a
		set_country_flag = heirs_khan_contestant
		tooltip = {
			create_point_of_interest = {
				id = marauder_rally_point
				name = heirs_khan_rally_point_name
				desc = heirs_khan_rally_point_desc
				event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate
				location = event_target:marauder_rally_point
			}
		}
    }

	option = {
		name = nomads.600.a # The AI go usurping the khanate, it wont be too different from the player perspective
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
	}
}

# A fleet has entered a system | See also: on_fleet_auto_move_arrival
# Scope = Fleet
# From = System
fleet_event = {
    id = nomads.605
    title = $TRANSMISSION$
    desc = nomads.605.desc
    is_triggered_only = yes
    trigger = {
        owner = {
            has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
			NOT = { has_country_flag = confronted_aspiring_khan }
        }
        solar_system = {
            any_fleet_in_system = {
                has_fleet_flag = aspiring_khan
            }
        }
    }
    diplomatic = yes
    picture_event_data = {
        portrait = event_target:khan_aspirant@root.owner
        room = khan_room
    }

    immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = confronted_aspiring_khan
			create_leader = {
				class = commander
				species = owner_main_species
				effect = {
					save_event_target_as = khan_aspirant@root.owner
					exile_leader_as = khan_aspirant
				}
			}
		}
        solar_system = {
            random_fleet_in_system = {
                limit = {
                    has_fleet_flag = aspiring_khan
                }
                save_event_target_as = aspiring_khan_fleet
				owner = {
					set_faction_hostility = {
						target = root.owner
						set_hostile = yes
						set_neutral = no
					}
				}
            }
        }
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = marauder_2_pledged }
			}
			event_target:marauder_country_2 = {
				create_fleet = {
					effect = {
						set_owner = prev
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Lancer" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Lancer" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						set_location = { target = root distance = 100 angle = 60 }
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
						set_aggro_range = 500
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_country_flag = marauder_3_pledged }
			}
			event_target:marauder_country_3 = {
				create_fleet = {
					effect = {
						set_owner = prev
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Outrider" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Lancer" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						create_ship = { name = random design = "NAME_Lancer" graphical_culture = "pirate_01" }
						set_location = { target = root distance = 100 angle = 120 }
						set_fleet_stance = aggressive
						set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
						set_aggro_range = 500
					}
				}
			}
		}
    }

	option = {
		name = nomads.605.a
	}
}

# This = owner of fleet 1 (combatant)
# From = owner of fleet 2 (destroyed)
# FromFrom = fleet 1
# FromFromFrom = fleet 2
country_event = { # You defeated the Khan Aspirant, time to be the Khan?
	id = nomads.610
	title = nomads.610.name
	desc = nomads.610.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_heirs_of_the_khan
	is_triggered_only = yes
	event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate

	trigger = {
		has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
		fromfromfrom = {
			OR = {
				has_fleet_flag = aspiring_khan
				AND = {
					owner? = { has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan }
					any_owned_ship = { is_capital = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			any_playable_country = {
				has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
				NOT = { is_same_value = root }
				is_ai = no
				NOT = { has_country_flag = won_khan_duel } # Previous winners who now have been defeated will have this flag
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = player_khan_imminent
		remove_global_flag = aspiring_khan_spawned
		set_country_flag = won_khan_duel
		from = { # Making sure to remove the Khan in Waiting flag from previous winners
			remove_country_flag = khan_in_waiting
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
				}
				country_event = { id = nomads.630 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "cannot_be_defender_of_the_galaxy"
				NOT = { has_ascension_perk = ap_defender_of_the_galaxy }
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "cannot_be_custodian"
				is_galactic_custodian = no
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = "cannot_be_gal_emperor"
				is_galactic_emperor = no
			}
		}
		name = nomads.610.a
		custom_tooltip = nomads.610.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			make_heirs_khan = yes
			play_sound = relic_activation_khans_throne
			save_event_target_as = this_country
			country_event = { id = timeline.130 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.610.b
		custom_tooltip = nomads.610.b.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			save_event_target_as = heirs_marauder_overlord
			set_country_flag = marauder_overlord
			set_country_flag = marauder_overlord_1
			event_target:marauder_country_1 = {
				set_faction_hostility = {
					target = root
					set_friendly = yes
				}
				country_event = { id = nomads.750 days = 720 random = 20 }
			}

		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.610.c
		custom_tooltip = nomads.610.c.tt
	}

	after = {
		add_relic = r_khans_throne
		end_event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate
	}
}

# This = owner of fleet 1 (combatant)
# From = owner of fleet 2 (destroyed)
# FromFrom = fleet 1
# FromFromFrom = fleet 2
country_event = { # You defeated the Khan Aspirant, but there is another player out there
	id = nomads.615
	title = nomads.610.name
	desc = nomads.615.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_heirs_of_the_khan
	is_triggered_only = yes

	event_chain = heirs_khan_candidate

	trigger = {
		has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
		NOT = { has_country_flag = won_khan_duel }
		fromfromfrom = {
			OR = {
				has_fleet_flag = aspiring_khan
				AND = {
					owner? = {
						has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
						has_country_flag = khan_in_waiting
					}
					any_owned_ship = { is_capital = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		any_playable_country = {
			has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
			NOT = { is_same_value = root }
			is_ai = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = won_khan_duel } # Previous winners who now have been defeated will have this flag
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = player_khan_imminent
		set_country_flag = won_khan_duel
		set_country_flag = khan_in_waiting
		from = { # Making sure to remove the Khan in Waiting flag from previous winners
			remove_country_flag = khan_in_waiting
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
				}
				country_event = { id = nomads.630 }
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = nomads.620
			years = 3
		}
		if = { #We remove the POIs from the winner
			limit = {
				has_point_of_interest = { poi = heirs_khan_in_waiting }
			}
			remove_point_of_interest = heirs_khan_in_waiting
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_point_of_interest = { poi = marauder_rally_point }
			}
			remove_point_of_interest = marauder_rally_point
		}
		every_playable_country = {
			limit = {
				has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
				NOR = {
					is_same_value = root
					has_country_flag = won_khan_duel
				}
			}
			if = { #And we remove them from the other countries
				limit = {
					has_point_of_interest = { poi = heirs_khan_in_waiting }
				}
				remove_point_of_interest = heirs_khan_in_waiting
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_point_of_interest = { poi = marauder_rally_point }
				}
				remove_point_of_interest = marauder_rally_point
			}
			country_event = { id = nomads.625 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.615.a
	}
}

# Your Khan died!
# This = Country
# From = Leader
country_event = {
	id = nomads.635
    title = nomads.635.name
    desc = nomads.635.desc
    picture = GFX_evt_khan_throne_room
    show_sound = event_shroud_song
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			has_trait = leader_trait_ruler_great_khan
			NOT = {
				has_leader_flag = leader_death_events_blocked

			}
		}
		has_country_flag = heir_of_the_khan_khan
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = heir_of_the_khan_khan_died
		event_target:marauder_country_1? = { # When your Khan dies you stop getting reinforcments and your vassal loses all the constructors
			every_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					is_ship_size = constructor
				}
				delete_fleet = this
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # We are done being the Khan
		name = nomads.635.a
		custom_tooltip = nomads.635.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_flag = heir_of_the_khan_khan
			restore_country_backup_data = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:marauder_country_1? = {
						count_system_within_border = {
							count > 0
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:marauder_country_1? = {
					if = { #First we check if you still have the original marauder systems
						limit = {
							any_system_within_border = {
								has_star_flag = marauder_capital_1
							}
						}
						random_system_within_border = {
							limit = {
								has_star_flag = marauder_capital_1
							}
							save_event_target_as = closest_system
							save_event_target_as = capital_system
						}
					}
					else = {
						random_system_within_border = {
							weights = {
								base = 5
								modifier = {
									factor = value:num_owned_neighbor_systems
									always = yes
								}
							}
							save_event_target_as = closest_system
							save_event_target_as = capital_system
						}
					}
					while = {
						count = value:twentyfive_percent_systems_min_5
						event_target:closest_system = {
							set_star_flag = heir_marauder_system
							if = {
								limit = {
									any_neighbor_system = {
										space_owner? = {
											is_same_value = event_target:marauder_country_1
										}
										NOT = { has_star_flag = heir_marauder_system }
									}
								}
								random_neighbor_system = {
									limit = {
										space_owner? = {
											is_same_value = event_target:marauder_country_1
										}
										NOT = { has_star_flag = heir_marauder_system }
									}
									save_event_target_as = closest_system
								}
							}
							else = {
								closest_system = {
									limit = {
										space_owner? = {
											is_same_value = event_target:marauder_country_1
										}
										NOT = { has_star_flag = heir_marauder_system }
									}
									save_event_target_as = closest_system
								}
							}
						}
					}
					change_country_flag = {
						icon = {
							category = "pirate"
							file = "flag_pirate_10.dds"
						}
						background = {
							category = "backgrounds"
							file = "00_solid.dds"
						}
						colors = {
							"black"
							"black"
							"null"
							"null"
						}
					}
					set_country_type = dormant_marauders
					remove_country_flag = heirs_of_khan_host
					every_system_within_border = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { has_star_flag = heir_marauder_system }
							}
							every_system_planet_colony = {
								limit = {
									owner? = {
										is_primitive = no
									}
								}
								destroy_colony = yes
							}
							starbase.fleet = {
								destroy_fleet = this
							}
						}
						else = {
							populate_heir_marauder_system_defenses = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_subject = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_origin = origin_nomadic_purger
					}
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					who = root
					modifier = opinion_liberated_us
				}
				add_trust = {
					who = root
					amount = 20
				}
				release_subject = yes
			}
			save_event_target_as = heirs_marauder_overlord
			set_country_flag = marauder_overlord
			set_country_flag = marauder_overlord_1
			event_target:marauder_country_1 = {
				country_event = { id = nomads.750 days = 720 random = 20 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # We will rule forever
		name = nomads.635.b
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = khans_forever
			days = -1
		}
	}
}

#Marauder Dividends
country_event = {
	id = nomads.750
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		event_target:heirs_marauder_overlord? = {
			is_forced_friendly = root # Checking you are still friendly to your Marauder
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		event_target:heirs_marauder_overlord = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {}
				2 = {
					create_message = {
						type = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS
						localization = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS_ENERGY_DESC
						days = @toast_message_days
						variable = {
							type = name
							localization = MARAUDER
							scope = root
						}
					}
					add_monthly_resource_mult = {
						resource = energy
						value = @tier3materialreward
						min = @tier3materialmin
						max = @tier3materialmax
					}
				}
				2 = {
					create_message = {
						type = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS
						localization = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS_FOOD_DESC
						days = @toast_message_days
						variable = {
							type = name
							localization = MARAUDER
							scope = root
						}
					}
					add_monthly_resource_mult = {
						resource = food
						value = @tier3materialreward
						min = @tier3materialmin
						max = @tier3materialmax
					}
				}
				2 = {
					create_message = {
						type = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS
						localization = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS_MINERALS_DESC
						days = @toast_message_days
						variable = {
							type = name
							localization = MARAUDER
							scope = root
						}
					}
					add_monthly_resource_mult = {
						resource = minerals
						value = @tier3materialreward
						min = @tier3materialmin
						max = @tier3materialmax
					}
				}
				2 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = block_reinforcements
					}
					root = {
						random_planet_within_border = {
							save_event_target_as = rally_point
						}
					}
					create_balanced_fleet = {
						name = "NAME_Hunting_Fleet"
						size = 125
						ship_designs = {
							NAME_Outrider
							NAME_Lancer
							NAME_Void_Champion
							NAME_Ancestral_Glory
						}
						effect = {
							set_owner = root #For ship names
							set_location = event_target:rally_point
							set_fleet_stance = aggressive
							set_fleet_bombardment_stance = indiscriminate
							set_aggro_range_measure_from = self
							set_aggro_range = 150
							give_fleet = { controller = prev days = 999999 }
							add_modifier = { modifier = marauder_friend_discount }
						}
					}
					create_message = {
						type = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS
						localization = HEIRS_DIVIDENDS_SHIPS_DESC
						days = @toast_message_days
						target = event_target:rally_point
						variable = {
							type = name
							localization = MARAUDER
							scope = root
						}
						variable = {
							type = name
							localization = PLANET
							scope = event_target:rally_point
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = nomads.750 days = 360 random = 30 }
	}
}

# Fired when a war begins for the Khan; sets the Host hostile to everyone fighting the Khan.
# Root = Country (war participant), From = War
country_event = {
	id = nomads.755
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = heir_of_the_khan_khan
		exists = event_target:marauder_country_1
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			every_war_participant = {
				limit = {
					is_at_war_with = root
				}
				set_country_flag = khan_war_enemy
				set_faction_hostility = {
					target = event_target:marauder_country_1
					set_hostile = yes
					set_neutral = no
					set_friendly = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Catches late-joiners who enter an existing Khan war via call-to-arms; on_war_beginning does not re-fire for them.
country_event = {
	id = nomads.756
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:great_khan
		exists = event_target:marauder_country_1
		is_at_war_with = event_target:great_khan
		NOR = {
			has_country_flag = khan_war_enemy
			has_country_flag = heir_of_the_khan_khan
			is_same_value = event_target:marauder_country_1
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = khan_war_enemy
		set_faction_hostility = {
			target = event_target:marauder_country_1
			set_hostile = yes
			set_neutral = no
			set_friendly = no
		}
	}
}

# Fired when a war ends or an ally peaces out; resets Host hostility for any flagged enemy the Khan is no longer fighting.
country_event = {
	id = nomads.760
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = event_target:great_khan
		exists = event_target:marauder_country_1
		any_country = {
			has_country_flag = khan_war_enemy
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = khan_war_enemy
				NOT = { is_at_war_with = event_target:great_khan }
			}
			remove_country_flag = khan_war_enemy
			set_faction_hostility = {
				target = event_target:marauder_country_1
				set_hostile = no
				set_neutral = yes
				set_friendly = no
			}
		}
	}
}

# Passenger Satisfaction situation start
# Fired by: on_game_start_country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1000
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
	}

	immediate = {
		start_situation = {
			type = situation_passenger_satisfaction
		}
	}
}

# Passenger Disembarkation -> Become a planet-bound non-nomad empire
# Fired by: situation on_first_enter
situation_event = {
	id = nomads.1005
	title = "nomads.1005.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = no
				is_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1005.regular.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1005.hive.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1005.machine.desc"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_big_landing_ship
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = forever_cruise_planetfall # This stops crew and passenger contracts from spawning
			every_issued_mission = {
				cancel_contract = {
					refund = no
					show_message = no
				}
			}
			every_owned_contract = {
				cancel_contract = {
					refund = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Regular
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = no
				is_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1005.regular.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1005.all.a.tt"
	}
	option = { # Hive
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1005.hive.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1005.all.a.tt"
	}
	option = { # Machine
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1005.machine.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1005.all.a.tt"
	}
}

	id = nomads.1025
	title = "nomads.1025.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = no
				is_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1025.regular.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1025.hive.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1025.machine.desc"
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_synthetic_empire = no }
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_surrender
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_synthetic_empire = yes }
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_organic_oppression
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = forever_cruise_mutiny # This stops crew and passenger contracts from spawning
			set_country_flag = free_government_reform
			every_issued_mission = {
				cancel_contract = {
					refund = no
					show_message = no
				}
			}
			every_owned_contract = {
				cancel_contract = {
					refund = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Regular
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = no
				is_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1025.regular.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1025.all.a.tt"
	}

			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1025.hive.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1025.all.a.tt"

				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1025.machine.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1025.all.a.tt"
	}
}

# Mutiny Completed
# Fired by: on_post_government_changed
# THIS = country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1030
	title = "nomads.1030.name"
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = no
				is_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1030.regular.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1030.hive.desc"
	}

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1030.machine_servitor.desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.1030.machine.desc"
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_synthetic_empire = no }
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_nomad_default
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_synthetic_empire = yes }
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_arkship_in_orbit
	}
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_mutiny
			NOT = { has_country_flag = forever_cruise_over }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_country_flag = forever_cruise_mutiny
		set_country_flag = forever_cruise_over
		remove_forever_cruise_citizenships = yes
		random_situation = {
			limit = { is_situation_type = situation_passenger_satisfaction }
			destroy_situation = this
		}
	}

	option = { # Regular
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = no
				is_machine_empire = no
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1030.regular.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1030.all.a.tt"
	}
	option = { # Hive
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1030.hive.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1030.all.a.tt"
	}
	option = { # Machine (Rogue Servitor → Determined Exterminator)
		exclusive_trigger = {
			owner = {
				has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1030.machine.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1030.machine_servitor.a.tt"
		hidden_effect = {
			force_remove_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			force_add_civic = civic_machine_terminator
		}
	}
	option = { # Machine
		trigger = {
			owner = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				NOT = {	has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
			}
		}
		name = "nomads.1030.machine.a"
		custom_tooltip = "nomads.1030.all.a.tt"
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			save_event_target_as = this_country
			country_event = { id = timeline.120 }
		}
	}
}

# Forever Cruise contract generation delayer
# Fired by: on_yearly_pulse_country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1300
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
		has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		NOR = {
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_planetfall
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_mutiny
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_over
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = nomads.1305 days = 15 random = 340 }
	}
}

# Forever Cruise passenger and crew contracts.
# Fired by: nomads.1300
# this = country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1305
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
		has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		count_issued_contracts < 3
		NOR = {
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_planetfall
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_mutiny
			has_country_flag = forever_cruise_over
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = nomad_country
		set_variable = { which = cruise_contract_attempts value = 0 }
		while = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = cruise_contract_issued }
				check_variable = { which = cruise_contract_attempts value < 5 }
			}
			change_variable = { which = cruise_contract_attempts value = 1 }

# Orun Veyth, The Revenant
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1505
	title = "nomads.1505.name"
	desc = "nomads.1505.desc"
	show_sound = nom_paragon_1_orun_veyth_the_revenant
	is_triggered_only = yes

	picture = GFX_leader_recruitment_bg_renowned
	auto_opens = no
	event_window_type = leader_recruit
	notification_event_icon = "GFX_message_leader_recruitment_revenant"

	immediate = {
		ethic_leader_creator = {
			SPECIES_CLASS = random_non_machine
			LEADER_PORTRAIT = par_renown_17
			CLASS = commander
			TIER = leader_tier_renowned
			NAME = NAME_nomadic_revenant
			LEVEL = 4
			GENDER = indeterminable
			IMMORTAL = no
			ETHIC = egalitarian
			DESC = DESC_nomadic_revenant
			CATCH_PHRASE = catch_phrase_nomadic_revenant
		}
		last_created_leader = {
			add_trait = {
				trait = subclass_commander_admiral
				consume_selection = yes
			}
			add_trait = {
				trait = leader_trait_unyielding
				consume_selection = yes
			}
			add_trait = {
				trait = leader_trait_artillerist
				consume_selection = yes
			}
			add_trait = {
				trait = leader_trait_volatile
				consume_selection = yes
			}
			add_trait = {
				trait = leader_trait_adaptable
				consume_selection = yes
			}
			add_trait = {
				trait = leader_trait_nomadic_revenant
				consume_selection = yes
			}
			set_age = 42
		}
	}

	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:ethic_leader
		room = ethic_spaceship_room
	}

	option = {
		name = DISMISS
		tag = dismiss_leader
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_global_flag = nomadic_revenant # Put this leader back into the pool, so player can still get them
			ethic_leader_kill_effect = yes
			set_country_flag = dismissed_nomadic_revenant
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nomads.1505.a
		response_text = nomads.1505.a.response
		is_dialog_only = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = nomads.1505.b
		response_text = nomads.1505.b.response
		is_dialog_only = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = nomads.1505.c
		response_text = nomads.1505.c.response
		is_dialog_only = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = nomads.1505.d
		response_text = nomads.1505.d.response
		is_dialog_only = yes
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			species_portrait = humanoid_02
		}
		name = nomads.1505.e
		response_text = nomads.1505.e.response
		is_dialog_only = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = HIRE
		tag = hire_leader
		custom_tooltip = nomads.1505.hire_custom_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			ethic_leader_hire_effect = {
				GLOBAL_EVENT_TARGET = nomadic_revenant
			}
			set_country_flag = hired_nomadic_revenant
			set_variable = {
				which = revenant_oath
				value = 1
			}
			set_global_flag = hired_nomadic_paragon_1
		}
	}
}

# Fired by on_fleet_destroyed_perp
# From = owner of fleet 2 (destroyed)
# FromFrom = fleet 1
# FromFromFrom = fleet 2
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1510
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_revenant
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = revenant_oath_flag
		}
		FromFrom.leader = {
			has_leader_flag = nomadic_revenant
		}
		from = {
			has_country_flag = first_pop_purged
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = razed_by_revenant
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = revenant_oath
					value = 4
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = revenant_oath_flag
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				which = revenant_oath
				value = 1
			}
		}
		from = {
			set_country_flag = razed_by_revenant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nomadic_revenant_first_revenge
				}
			}
			set_country_flag =  nomadic_revenant_first_revenge
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1511
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1512
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hidden Event to spawn Sero's pre-sapients after hiring
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1522
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = found_presapients
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = found_presapients
		}
		capital_scope = {
			save_event_target_as = pre_sapient_planet
			spawn_presapient_species_randomizer_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

# Hidden Event to trigger Leader UI Popup and a Toast Thereafter
# Fired by on_survey_planet
# Scope = Ship
# From = Planet
ship_event = {
	id = nomads.1524
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = leader
		leader = {
			has_leader_flag = nomadic_naturalist
		}
		from = {
			any_owned_pop_group = {
				is_sapient = no
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			random_owned_pop_group = {
				limit = {
					is_sapient = no
				}
				save_event_target_as = nomadic_naturalist_presapients
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = nomadic_naturalist_first_presapients
					}
				}
				set_country_flag =  nomadic_naturalist_first_presapients
				country_event = {
					id = nomads.1525
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = nomads.1526
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hidden Event to improve trait buffs; triggers Leader UI Popup and a Toast Thereafter
# Fired by nomads.3002 (Contract Completed)
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1535
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = caregiver_contract_flag
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = caregiver_contracts_completed
					value = 5
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = caregiver_contract_flag
		}
		else = {
			change_variable = {
				which = caregiver_contracts_completed
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = first_creche
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = first_creche
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1545
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1550
			}
		}
	}
}

# Trigger Event for Champion Trophies
# Fired by on_colony_attackers_win
# This = country, lead attacker
# From = country, colony owner
# FromFrom = colony
country_event = {
	id = nomads.1556
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		FromFrom = {
			NOT = {
				planet = { has_carrier_flag = invaded_by_champion }
			}
		}
		has_country_flag = hired_nomadic_champion
		FromFrom = {
			any_ground_combat_attacker = {
				leader? = {
					has_leader_flag = nomadic_champion
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		FromFrom = {
			planet = { set_carrier_flag = invaded_by_champion }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = champion_trophies_collected
					value < 7
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					# Nothing Happens
				}
				1 = { # Trophy Found
					change_variable = {
						which = champion_trophies_collected
						value = 1
					}
					country_event = {
						id = nomads.1560 # Trophy Acquired event
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				id = nomads.1565
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1570
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hidden event determines if the first POI successfully triggers the princess' memories, fired by on_entering_system_fleet
# from = system
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.1590
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			has_star_flag = princess_poi_system
		}
		owner = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = princess_poi_first_memory
			}
			any_owned_leader = {
				has_leader_flag = nomadic_princess
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						has_carrier_flag = princess_poi_planet_1
					}
				}
				root.owner = {
					remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_1
				}
				remove_star_flag = princess_poi_system
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						has_carrier_flag = princess_poi_planet_2
					}
				}
				root.owner = {
					remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_2
				}
				remove_star_flag = princess_poi_system
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						has_carrier_flag = princess_poi_planet_3
					}
				}
				root.owner = {
					remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_3
				}
				remove_star_flag = princess_poi_system
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = princess_poi_still_forgets
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					75 = {
						country_event = {
							id = nomads.1595
						}
					}
					25 = {
						set_country_flag = princess_poi_first_memory
						country_event = {
							id = nomads.1600
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = princess_poi_first_memory
				country_event = {
					id = nomads.1600
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		text = nomads.1600.human
	}

	event_chain = nomadic_princess_chain
	show_sound = event_arkship_bridge

	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.1600.a
	}
	option = {
		name = nomads.1600.b
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_1
			remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_2
			remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_3
			random_system = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_star_flag = princess_poi_system
					}

						is_star_class = sc_black_hole
						is_inside_nebula = yes
					}
				}
				star = {
					create_ambient_object = {
						type = ambient_arkship_destroyed
					}
					last_created_ambient_object = {
						set_location = {
							target = prev
							distance = 20
							angle = random
						}
						save_event_target_as = seralune_throne
					}
				}
			}
		}
		enable_special_project = {
			name = "NOMADIC_PRINCESS_SPECIAL_PROJECT"
			location = event_target:seralune_throne
			owner = ROOT
		}
	}
}

# The player has chosen to investigate further; fired by on_entering_system_fleet
# from = system
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.1605
	title = nomads.1605.name
	desc = nomads.1605.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_arkship_bridge
	event_chain = nomadic_princess_chain
	show_sound = event_arkship_bridge
	location = from

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			has_star_flag = princess_poi_system
		}
		owner = {
			has_country_flag = princess_poi_first_memory
			NOR = {
				has_country_flag = princess_poi_still_forgets
				has_country_flag = princess_poi_second_memory
			}
			any_owned_leader = {
				has_leader_flag = nomadic_princess
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = princess_poi_second_memory
		}
		from = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						has_carrier_flag = princess_poi_planet_1
					}
				}
				root.owner = {
					remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_1
				}
				remove_star_flag = princess_poi_system
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						has_carrier_flag = princess_poi_planet_2
					}
				}
				root.owner = {
					remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_2
				}
				remove_star_flag = princess_poi_system
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_system_planet = {
						has_carrier_flag = princess_poi_planet_3
					}
				}
				root.owner = {
					remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_3
				}
				remove_star_flag = princess_poi_system
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.1605.a
		owner = {
			random_owned_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_leader_flag = nomadic_princess
				}
				add_experience = 1500
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = princess_poi_still_forgets
					has_country_flag = princess_poi_first_memory
				}
				has_country_flag = princess_poi_second_memory
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = princess_poi_every_memory
			}
			any_owned_leader = {
				has_leader_flag = nomadic_princess
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = princess_poi_every_memory
		}
		random_system = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_star_flag = princess_poi_system
				}
				distance = {
					source = fromfrom
					min_jumps = 5
				}
				OR = {
					is_star_class = sc_black_hole
					is_inside_nebula = yes
				}
			}
			set_star_flag = nomadic_princess_star
			star = {
				create_ambient_object = {
					type = ambient_arkship_destroyed
				}
				last_created_ambient_object = {
					set_location = {
						target = prev
						distance = 20
						angle = random
					}

				}
			}
		}
	}

		name = nomads.1610.a

			random_owned_leader = {

					has_leader_flag = nomadic_princess

		}

			owner = {
				remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_1
				remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_2
				remove_point_of_interest = nomadic_princess_poi_3
			}
		}
	}
}

ship_event = {
	id = nomads.1625
	title = nomads.1625.name
	desc = nomads.1625.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_arkship_in_orbit
	event_chain = nomadic_princess_chain
	show_sound = event_celebration
	location = from
	event_window_type = leader_story

	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:nomadic_princess
		room = root.owner
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_technology = tech_civilian_arkship
					}
				}
				give_technology = {
					tech = tech_civilian_arkship
				}
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = "NAME_princess_fleet"
				effect = {
					set_owner = prev
					set_location = event_target:seralune_throne
					create_ship = {
						name = "NAME_princess_ship"
						random_existing_design = civilian_arkship_tier_1
						effect = {
							save_event_target_as = nomadic_princess_ship
							set_ship_flag = nomadic_princess_ship
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:seralune_throne = {
			destroy_ambient_object = this
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.1625.a
	}

	after = {
		owner = {
			end_event_chain = nomadic_princess_chain
			remove_country_flag = hired_nomadic_princess
			set_country_flag = princess_can_die
		}
	}
}

# Non-nomad AI contract generation delayer
# Fired by: on_yearly_pulse_country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3000
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = nomads.3001 days = 15 random = 340 }
	}
}

# Non-nomad AI contract issuer
# Fired by: nomads.3000
# this = country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
		can_issue_contracts_trigger = yes
		any_relation = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_communications = prev
			NOT = {
				is_at_war_with = prev
			}
			root = { #check that ai likes at least one nomad enough
				opinion_level = {
					who = prev
					level >= neutral
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						count_country = {
							count >= 15
							limit = { is_country_type = default }
						}
					}
					count_issued_contracts = 0
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						count_country = {
							count >= 10
							limit = { is_country_type = default }
						}
					}
					count_issued_contracts <= 1
				}
				else = {
					count_issued_contracts <= 2
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { # Chance of nothing
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						is_xenophobe = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 5
						is_fanatic_xenophobe = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_civic = civic_pompous_purists
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 4
						is_gestalt = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						is_megacorp = yes
					}
				}
				20 = { # Harvest
					modifier = { # skip if a harvest contract is already issued/picked up
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = harvest_contract_active
					}
					modifier = { #more likely if deficit
						factor = 5
						OR = {
							has_deficit = minerals
							has_deficit = energy
							has_deficit = alloys
							has_deficit = exotic_gases
							has_deficit = rare_crystals
							has_deficit = volatile_motes
						}
					}
					random_system_within_border = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_star_flag = issued_harvest_contract
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_modifier = harvested_resources_mining
								}
							}
							if = {
								limit = {
									root = {
										has_deficit = exotic_gases
									}
									any_system_planet = {
										is_star = no
										has_resource = {
											type = exotic_gases
											amount > 0
										}
									}
								}
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_resource = {
										type = exotic_gases
										amount > 0
									}
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									root = {
										has_deficit = rare_crystals
									}
									any_system_planet = {
										is_star = no
										has_resource = {
											type = rare_crystals
											amount > 0
										}
									}
								}
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_resource = {
										type = rare_crystals
										amount > 0
									}
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									root = {
										has_deficit = volatile_motes
									}
									any_system_planet = {
										is_star = no
										has_resource = {
											type = volatile_motes
											amount > 0
										}
									}
								}
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_resource = {
										type = volatile_motes
										amount > 0
									}
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									root = {
										has_deficit = minerals
									}
									any_system_planet = {
										is_star = no
										has_resource = {
											type = minerals
											amount > 0
										}
									}
								}
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_resource = {
										type = minerals
										amount > 0
									}
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									root = {
										has_deficit = energy
									}
									any_system_planet = {
										is_star = no
										has_resource = {
											type = energy
											amount > 0
										}
									}
								}
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_resource = {
										type = energy
										amount > 0
									}
								}
							}
							else_if = {
								limit = {
									root = {
										has_deficit = alloys
									}
									any_system_planet = {
										is_star = no
										has_resource = {
											type = alloys
											amount > 0
										}
									}
								}
								any_system_planet = {
									is_star = no
									has_resource = {
										type = alloys
										amount > 0
									}
								}
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = contract_system
						#Resource Type picker
						random_list = {
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = minerals
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = energy
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = consumer_goods
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = alloys
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = volatile_motes
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = exotic_gases
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = rare_crystals
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = sr_living_metal
							}
							inline_script = {
								script = contracts/AIHarvestOption
								RESOURCE = nanites
							}
						}
						set_timed_star_flag = {
							flag = issued_harvest_contract
							days = 1800
						}
					}
				}
				10 = { # Espionage
					modifier = { # skip if an espionage support contract is already issued/picked up
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = espionage_support_contract_active
					}
					modifier = { #check for valid spynets
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							any_spynetwork = {
								NOT = { has_spynetwork_flag = issued_spy_support_contract }
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							any_envoy = {
								has_envoy_task = {
									task = spy_network
								}
							}
						}
					}
					#reduced for nice guys
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						NOT = { has_tradition = tr_subterfuge_adopt }
						is_xenophile = yes
						has_civic = civic_warrior_culture #tis dishonorable
						has_origin = origin_heirs_of_the_khan
					}
					#increases for sneaky people
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.5
						OR = {
							has_civic = civic_cutthroat_politics
							has_civic = civic_shadow_council
							has_civic = civic_secret_societies
							has_civic = civic_criminal_heritage
							has_civic = civic_secret_societies_corporate
							has_civic = civic_hive_bodysnatcher
							has_civic = civic_hive_familiar_face
							has_civic = civic_machine_spybots
						}
					}
					#increased for weak empire
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_country_type = default #don't count FE's
							relative_power = {
								who = root
								category = all
								value = overwhelming
							}
						}
					}

					random_spynetwork = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_spynetwork_flag = issued_spy_support_contract }
							has_spy_power > 9
							target = { is_country_type = default }
						}
						save_event_target_as = espionage_support_spynetwork
						target = { save_event_target_as = espionage_support_target }
						random_list = {
							10 = {
								modifier = { #always a chance for simple contract
									factor = 0.1
									target = {
										num_owned_planets > 3
									}
								}
								create_espionage_contract = { CONTRACT = contract_espionage_support }
							}
							10 = {
								modifier = {
									factor = 0
									target = {
										OR = {
											num_owned_planets < 3
											num_owned_planets > 7
										}
									}
								}
								create_espionage_contract = { CONTRACT = contract_espionage_support_2 }
							}
							10 = {
								modifier = {
									factor = 0
									target = {
										OR = {
											num_owned_planets < 7
											num_owned_planets > 13
										}
									}
								}
								create_espionage_contract = { CONTRACT = contract_espionage_support_3 }
							}
							10 = {
								modifier = {
									factor = 0
									target = {
										num_owned_planets <= 13
									}
								}
								create_espionage_contract = { CONTRACT = contract_espionage_support_4 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				20 = { # Deep Scan
					modifier = { # skip if a deep scan contract is already issued/picked up
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = deep_scan_contract_active
					}
					modifier = { #increased for materialists and explorers
						factor = 2
						OR = {
							is_materialist = yes
							has_tradition = tr_discovery_adopt
							has_civic = civic_eager_explorers
							has_civic = civic_hive_stargazers
							has_civic = civic_privatized_exploration
							has_civic = civic_machine_exploration_protocol
						}
					}
					modifier = { #increased if boxed in -won't catch all edge cases like xenophobe FE or leviathans, but good enough.
						factor = 3
						NOT = {
							any_system_within_border = {
								any_neighbor_system = {
									NOT = { exists = owner }
								}
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = { #decrease if everything that can be deep scanned has been deep scanned
						factor = 0.25
						NOT = {
							any_planet_within_border = {
								has_anomaly = no
								is_artificial = no
								is_ringworld = no
								NOT = {
									is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar
								}
								if = {
									limit = {
										habitable_planet = yes
									}
									root = {
										any_owned_leader = {
											has_leader_flag = nomadic_naturalist
										}
									}
								}
								NOT = { is_variable_set = times_deep_scanned }
							}
						}
					}
					modifier = { #blocked if no possible contractor
						factor = 0
						NOT = {
							any_relation = {
								is_nomadic = yes
								has_communications = prev
								has_deep_scan_capability = yes
							}
						}
					}
					random_system_within_border = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_star_flag = issued_deep_scan_contract }
						}
						save_event_target_as = contract_system
						owner = {
							issue_contract = {
								contract = contract_deep_scan
								location = event_target:contract_system
							}
							prev = {
								set_timed_star_flag = {
									flag = issued_deep_scan_contract
									days = 3600
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				5 = { # Raid Planet
					modifier = { # skip if a raid planet contract is already issued/picked up
						factor = 0
						has_country_flag = raid_planet_contract_active
					}
					modifier = { #check for valid targets (rival or war)
						factor = 0
						num_rivals < 1
						count_war = {
							count < 1
						}
					}
					#reduced for pacifists
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						is_pacifist = yes
					}
					#increased for militarists
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						is_militarist = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						is_fanatic_militarist = yes
					}
					#increased for weaker empires
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						any_neighbor_country = {
							is_country_type = default #don't count FE's
							OR = {
								is_rival = root
								is_at_war_with = root
							}
							relative_power = {
								who = root
								category = all
								value >= superior
							}
						}
					}
					#increased for enmity empires
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						has_tradition = tr_enmity_adopt
					}

					#War Case (takes priority over being petty)
					if = {
						limit = {
							count_war = {
								count < 0
							}
						}
						ordered_country = {
							limit = {
								is_at_war_with = root
							}
							position = 0
							order_by = fleet_power
							save_event_target_as = raid_target
							random_owned_planet = {
								save_event_target_as = contract_planet
							}
						}
						issue_contract = {
							contract = contract_raid_planet_small
							location = event_target:contract_planet
						}
					}
					#Rival Case
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							num_rivals > 0
						}
						random_rival_country = {
							limit = {
								is_country_type = default
							}
							save_event_target_as = raid_target
							random_owned_planet = {
								save_event_target_as = contract_planet
							}
						}
						issue_contract = {
							contract = contract_raid_planet_small

# Contract Completed, increment variable
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3002
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_set = contract_completed
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = contract_completed
				value = 1
			}
		}
        else = {
          set_variable = {
            which = contract_completed
            value = 1
          }
       }
	   if = { # Nomadic Caregiver Trait Effect
			limit = {
				any_owned_leader = {
					has_trait = leader_trait_nomadic_caregiver
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.1535
				days = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

# Forever Cruise Contract Completed, increment variable
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3003
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_variable_set = cruise_contract_completed
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = cruise_contract_completed
				value = 1
			}
		}
        else = {
          set_variable = {
            which = cruise_contract_completed
            value = 1
          }
       }
	}
}

# Non-nomad AI contract generation delayer
# Fired by: on_yearly_pulse_country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3005
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = nomads.3010 days = 15 random = 340 }
	}
}

# Nomads issue contracts for themselves. - DISABLED FOR NOW
# Fired by: on_yearly_pulse_country
# this = country
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3010
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		always = no
		is_nomadic = yes
		NOT = { has_origin = origin_forever_cruise }
	}

	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = nomad_country
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_communications = 0
				count_available_contracts = 0
			}

			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					is_arkship_fleet = yes
				}
				solar_system = {
					save_event_target_as = arkship_system
				}
			}

			event_target:nomad_country = {
				random_list = {
					1 = {
						inline_script = {
							script = events/nomads_find_resource_internal_event
							RESOURCE = minerals
						}
					}
					1 = {
						inline_script = {
							script = events/nomads_find_resource_internal_event
							RESOURCE = energy
						}
					}
					1 = {
						inline_script = {
							script = events/nomads_find_resource_internal_event
							RESOURCE = alloys
						}
					}
					1 = {
						inline_script = {
							script = events/nomads_scientific_observation_internal_event
							RESOURCE = physics_research
						}
					}
					1 = {
						inline_script = {
							script = events/nomads_scientific_observation_internal_event
							RESOURCE = engineering_research
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

planet_event = { # Raid Contract bombardement damage tracker - from on_planet_bombarded
	id = nomads.3015
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_event_chain = contract_raid_planet_chain
		}
		owner = { has_country_flag = raid_target@from }
	}

	immediate = {
		set_carrier_flag = raid_contract_planet@from
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
			trigger = planet_devastation
			variable = bomba
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_variable_set = bombatrack }
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = planet_devastation
				variable = bombatrack
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable_arithmetic = {
					which = bomba
					subtract = bombatrack
					value >= 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = bombatrack
				value = 1
			}
			from = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = contract_raid_planet_small
					counter = contract_progress_counter
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Megastructure Support Contract
# Root = Country
# From = System
# FromFrom = Fleet

country_event = { #AIs auto issue a contract when first building a new Megastructure (with a 5 year cooldown )
	id = nomads.3025
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		exists = from
		is_ai = yes
		can_issue_contracts_trigger = yes
		any_relation = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_communications = prev
			NOT = {
				is_at_war_with = prev
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = issued_megastructure_contract }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			issue_contract = {
				contract = contract_megastructure_support
				location = from
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = issued_megastructure_contract days = 1800 }
		}
	}
}

# Diplomatic Support

fleet_event = { #pick up delegates event and destination poi creation
	id = nomads.3036
	title = "nomads.3036.name"
	desc = { #has_communications
		trigger = {
			event_target:pickup_planet = {
				owner = {
					has_communications = root.owner
				}
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.3036.desc"
	}
	desc = {#no communications
		trigger = {
			event_target:pickup_planet = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { has_communications = root.owner }
				}
			}
		 }
		text = "nomads.3036.desc.nocomm"
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_tradedeal
	show_sound = event_hand_shake

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_event_chain = contract_diplomatic_support_chain
		}
		solar_system = {
			any_system_planet = {
				has_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_pickup_planet@root.owner
			}
		}
		is_arkship_fleet = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		solar_system = {
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = {
					has_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_pickup_planet@root.owner
				}
				save_event_target_as = pickup_planet
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							NOT = {
								has_communications = root.owner
							}
						}
					}
					owner = { establish_communications = root.owner }
				}
			}
		}
		set_fleet_flag = carrying_delegates
		random_galaxy_planet = {
			limit = {
				has_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_dropoff_planet@root.owner
			}
			save_event_target_as = dropoff_planet
		}

		owner = {
			remove_point_of_interest = diplomatic_support_pickup_poi@this
			remove_point_of_interest = diplomatic_support_destination_poi@this
			create_point_of_interest = {
				id = diplomatic_support_dropoff_poi@this
				name = "diplomatic_support_dropoff_poi_name"
				desc = diplomatic_support_dropoff_poi_desc
				event_chain = contract_diplomatic_support_chain
				location = event_target:dropoff_planet
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				abort_special_project = {
					type = CONTRACT_DIPLOMATIC_SUPPORT_TRAVEL_PROJECT
					location = event_target:pickup_planet.solar_system
				}
				enable_special_project = {
					name = "CONTRACT_DIPLOMATIC_SUPPORT_TRAVEL_PROJECT"
					location = event_target:dropoff_planet.solar_system
					owner = this
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.3036.a
		custom_tooltip = contract_dropoff_planet_tt
	}
}

fleet_event = { #Delegate destination check - From on_fleet_enter_system
	id = nomads.3045
	title = "nomads.3045.name"
	desc = "nomads.3045.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_diplomatic_visit
	show_sound = event_hand_shake

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_event_chain = contract_diplomatic_support_chain
		}
		solar_system = {
			any_system_planet = {
				has_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_dropoff_planet@root.owner
			}
		}
		is_arkship_fleet = yes
		has_fleet_flag = carrying_delegates
	}

	immediate = {
		random_galaxy_planet = {
			limit = {
				has_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_pickup_planet@root.owner
			}
			remove_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_pickup_planet@root.owner
			owner = {
				save_event_target_as = diplomatic_support_issuer
			}
		}
		solar_system = {
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = { has_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_dropoff_planet@root.owner }
				remove_carrier_flag = diplomatic_support_dropoff_planet@root.owner
				owner = {
					save_event_target_as = diplomatic_support_target
				}
			}
		}
		remove_fleet_flag = carrying_delegates
		random_list = {
			1 = { #meh success
				event_target:diplomatic_support_issuer = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						modifier = opinion_diplomacy_contract_small
						who = event_target:diplomatic_support_target
					}
					add_trust = {
						amount = 5
						who = event_target:diplomatic_support_target
					}
				}
			}
			3 = { #sucess
				event_target:diplomatic_support_issuer = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						modifier = opinion_diplomacy_contract
						who = event_target:diplomatic_support_target
					}
					add_trust = {
						amount = 10
						who = event_target:diplomatic_support_target
					}
				}
			}
			1 = { #great success
				event_target:diplomatic_support_issuer = {
					add_opinion_modifier = {
						modifier = opinion_diplomacy_contract_large
						who = event_target:diplomatic_support_target
					}
					add_trust = {
						amount = 15
						who = event_target:diplomatic_support_target
					}
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:diplomatic_support_target = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_diplomacy_contract
				who = event_target:diplomatic_support_issuer
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		owner = {
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_diplomatic_support
				counter = contract_diplomatic_support_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Prisoner Disposal
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3050
	title = "nomads.3050.name"
	desc = "nomads.3050.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_experimental_testing
	show_sound = event_criminal_activity

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			has_event_chain = contract_prisoner_disposal_chain
		}
		solar_system = {
			any_system_planet = {
				has_carrier_flag = prisoner_disposal_pickup_planet@root.owner
			}
		}
		is_arkship_fleet = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		solar_system = {
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = {
					has_carrier_flag = prisoner_disposal_pickup_planet@root.owner
				}
				save_event_target_as = pickup_planet
			}
		}
		random_owned_ship = {
			colony = {
				save_event_target_as = arkship
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#well drop them off later
		name = nomads.3050.a
		#flag fleet for scripted action
		custom_tooltip = transporting_prisoners_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_fleet_flag = transporting_prisoners
		}
		#add crime modifier
		event_target:arkship = {
			add_modifier = { #add crime mod to planet
				modifier = nomad_criminals_on_board
				years = 10
			}
		}
		#Can't choose this if awe already have another contract action
		trigger = {
			has_contract_scripted_action = no
		}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	#other options finish the contract there
	option = {#keep em ourselves
		name = nomads.3050.b
		trigger = {
			owner = { is_slaver = no }
		}
		owner = {
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_prisoner_disposal
				counter = contract_prisoner_disposal_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
		#add crime modifier
		event_target:arkship = {
			add_modifier = { #add crime mod to planet
				modifier = nomad_criminals_on_board
				years = 10
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #keep em ourselves (slaver)
		name = nomads.3050.c
		trigger = {
			event_target:pickup_planet.owner = { is_slaver = yes }
		}
		#no crime modifier for this one, you just get the pops
		owner = {
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_prisoner_disposal
				counter = contract_prisoner_disposal_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #keep and free them
		name = nomads.3050.d
		owner = {
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_prisoner_disposal
				counter = contract_prisoner_disposal_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { #add reduced crime modifier
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					event_target:pickup_planet.owner = {
						OR = {
							is_xenophile = yes #They're actually not that bad
							is_authoritarian = yes #They were actually unjustly jailed
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					root.owner = {
						has_valid_civic = civic_civil_education
					}
				}
				event_target:arkship = {
					add_modifier = { #add crime mod to planet
						modifier = nomad_reformed_criminals_on_board
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
			1 = { #add worse crime modifier
				modifier = {
					factor = 3
					event_target:pickup_planet.owner = {
						OR = {
							has_valid_civic = civic_void_reavers
							has_valid_civic = civic_criminal_heritage
							has_valid_civic = civic_hive_bodysnatcher
							has_valid_civic = civic_barbaric_despoilers
							has_ascension_perk = ap_nihilistic_acquisition
							is_xenophobe = yes
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:arkship = {
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = nomad_criminals_loose_on_board
						years = 5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:pickup_planet = {
				add_modifier = { #add anti crime mod to planet
					modifier = nomad_criminal_disposal
					years = 10
				}
				#transfer pop if applicable
				random_owned_pop_group = {
					weights = {
						base = 1
						modifier = {
							factor = 1000
							pop_group_size >= 300
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = source_pop_group
					if = {
						limit = {
							root.event_target:arkship = {
								has_modifier = nomad_reformed_criminals_on_board
							}
						}
						root.event_target:arkship = {
							create_pop_group = {
								pop_group = event_target:source_pop_group
								size = 0
								effect = {
									transfer_pop_amount = {
										source = event_target:source_pop_group
										target = this
										amount = 300
									}
									save_event_target_as = resettled_pop_group
								}
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						root.event_target:arkship = {
							create_pop_group = {
								pop_group = event_target:source_pop_group
								size = 0
								category = criminal
								effect = {
									transfer_pop_amount = {
										source = event_target:source_pop_group
										target = this
										amount = 300
									}
									save_event_target_as = resettled_pop_group
									set_pop_group_flag = criminal_pops
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				remove_carrier_flag = prisoner_disposal_pickup_planet@root.owner
			}
		}
	}
}

				limit = { is_mission_type = contract_prisoner_disposal }
