					save_event_target_as = prisoner_disposal_issuer
				}
			}
		}
		from = {
			remove_fleet_flag = transporting_prisoners
			fleet_event = { id = nomads.3052 }
		}
	}
}

fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3052
	title = "nomads.3052.name"
	desc = "nomads.3052.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_experimental_testing
	show_sound = event_criminal_activity

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Good riddance
		name = 03_RECALL_EMBASSY_HOSTILE
		random_owned_ship = {
			colony = {
				remove_modifier = nomad_criminals_on_board
				custom_tooltip = prisoner_tranfer_tt
				hidden_effect = {
					random_owned_pop_group = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								is_species = owner_main_species
								is_subspecies = owner_main_species
							}
						}
						weights = {
							base = 1
							modifier = {
								factor = 1000
								has_pop_group_flag = criminal_pops
							}
						}
						resettle_pop_group = {
							POP_GROUP = this
							PLANET = from
							AMOUNT = 300
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			from = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							is_gestalt = no
						}
						NOT = {
							has_modifier = penal_colony
							has_modifier = slave_colony
							is_planet_class = pc_cosmogenesis_world
						}
					}
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = nomad_criminals_dropped_off
						years = 10
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			fleet_event = { id = nomads.3053 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3053
	title = "nomads.3053.name"
	desc = {	# No problems
		text = "nomads.3053.desc"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer
				has_fleet_flag = detected
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {	# issuer problems
		text = "nomads.3053.desc.issuer.problem"
		trigger = {
			has_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer
		}
	}
	desc = {	# Yes problems
		text = "nomads.3053.desc.problem"
		trigger = {
			has_fleet_flag = detected
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_experimental_testing
	show_sound = event_criminal_activity

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				fromfrom.owner = {
					is_gestalt = no
				}
				fromfrom = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = penal_colony
						has_modifier = slave_colony
						is_planet_class = pc_cosmogenesis_world
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { #detected
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						owner = {
							relative_encryption_decryption = {
								target = event_target:prisoner_disposal_issuer
								value > 1
							}
						}
					}
					if = { #by issuer?
						limit = {
							fromfrom.owner? = {
								is_same_value = event_target:prisoner_disposal_issuer
							}
						}
						set_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer

					}
					else = { #not by issuer
						set_fleet_flag = detected
					}

				}
				1 = { #sneaky
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.1
						owner = {
							relative_encryption_decryption = {
								target = event_target:prisoner_disposal_issuer
								value < 1
							}
						}
					}
					#we just don't add a flag
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #detected
		name = UNFORTUNATE
		trigger = {
			has_fleet_flag = detected
		}
		from.owner = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_dropped_off_prisoners
				who = root.owner
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #issuer detected
		name = UNFORTUNATE
		trigger = {
			has_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer
		}
		#big opinion loss and contract cancel
		fromfrom.owner = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_dropped_off_our_prisoners
				who = root.owner
			}
		}
		owner = {
			random_owned_contract = {
				limit = {
					is_mission_type = contract_prisoner_disposal
				}
				cancel_contract = {
					refund = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EXCELLENT
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer
				has_fleet_flag = detected
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		#if not detected by issuer flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer }
			}
			owner = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = contract_prisoner_disposal
					counter = contract_prisoner_disposal_counter
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		#flag cleanup
		remove_fleet_flag = detected_by_issuer
		remove_fleet_flag = detected
	}
}

# Build Waystation Contract Complete
# Fired when a Waystation is constructed
# Fired by: on_waystation_built
# this = galactic object/solar system
# from = waystation owner
# fromfrom = waystation starbase
system_event = {
	id = nomads.3054
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_event_chain = contract_build_waystation_chain
		}
		has_star_flag = waystation_contract_system@root
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = build_waystation_complete
		}
		from = {
			# Gate the contract's abort trigger: marks "success is in flight" so the
			# any_fleet_in_system { is_waystation_ship } check on the next daily tick
			# doesn't race ahead of the counter-based success check.
			set_country_flag = build_waystation_contract_succeeded
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_build_waystation
				counter = contract_build_waystation_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

	trigger = {

			has_fleet_flag = pest_contract_target@root
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		add_mission_counter = {
			mission = contract_pest_control
			counter = contract_pest_control_counter
			amount = 1
		}

	}
}

# Sightseeing Tour - Check if Arkship has entered the system to pick up tourists
# Fired by: on_entering_system_fleet
# A fleet has entered a system
# Scope = Fleet
# From = System
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3060
	title = "nomads.3060.name"
	desc = "nomads.3060.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_obelisk_tourists
	show_sound = event_announcement
	location = root.solar_system
	event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
		}
		is_arkship_fleet = yes
		from = {
			has_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_start_system@root.owner
			NOT = { has_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_tourists_picked_upp@root.owner }
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			set_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_tourists_picked_upp@root.owner
		}
		set_fleet_flag = sightseeing_tour_arkship
		random_system = {
			limit = {
				distance = {
					source = prev.from
					use_bypasses = no
					min_jumps = 3
					max_jumps = 5
				}
				NOR = {
					has_star_flag = guardian
					has_star_flag = hostile_system
				}
			}
			weights = {
				base = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 10
					OR = {
						is_star_class = sc_black_hole
						is_star_class = sc_neutron_star
						is_star_class = sc_pulsar
					}
				}
			}
			set_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_destination_system@root.owner
			save_event_target_as = sightseeing_tour_destination_system
		}
		owner = {
			remove_point_of_interest = sightseeing_tour_start_poi
			create_point_of_interest = {
				id = sightseeing_tour_destination_poi
				name = "sightseeing_tour_destination_poi_name"
				desc = "sightseeing_tour_destination_poi_desc"
				event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
				location = event_target:sightseeing_tour_destination_system
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				abort_special_project = {
					type = CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_TRAVEL_PROJECT
					location = from
				}
				enable_special_project = {
					name = "CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_TRAVEL_PROJECT"
					location = event_target:sightseeing_tour_destination_system
					owner = this
				}
			}
			create_message = {
				type = MESSAGE_CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_START
				localization = MESSAGE_CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_START_LOCATION_DESC
				days = 30
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = SYSTEM
					scope = event_target:sightseeing_tour_destination_system
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.3060.a
		custom_tooltip = nomads.3060.a.tt
	}
}

# Sightseeing Tour - Check if Arkship has entered the system for tourists to sightsee
# Fired by: on_entering_system_fleet
# A fleet has entered a system
# Scope = Fleet
# From = System
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3065
	title = "nomads.3065.name"
	desc = "nomads.3065.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_space_funeral
	show_sound = evn_ove_obelisk_tourists
	location = root.solar_system
	event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
		}
		from = {
			has_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_destination_system@root.owner
		}
		has_fleet_flag = sightseeing_tour_arkship
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			remove_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_destination_system@root.owner
		}
		random_system = {
			limit = {
				has_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_start_system@root.owner
			}
			remove_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_start_system@root.owner
			set_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_end_system@root.owner
			save_event_target_as = sightseeing_tour_end_system
		}
		owner = {
			remove_point_of_interest = sightseeing_tour_destination_poi
			create_point_of_interest = {
				id = sightseeing_tour_end_poi
				name = "sightseeing_tour_end_poi_name"
				desc = "sightseeing_tour_end_poi_desc"
				event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
				location = event_target:sightseeing_tour_end_system
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				abort_special_project = {
					type = CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_TRAVEL_PROJECT
					location = from
				}
				enable_special_project = {
					name = "CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_TRAVEL_PROJECT"
					location = event_target:sightseeing_tour_end_system
					owner = this
				}
			}
			create_message = {
				type = MESSAGE_CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_END
				localization = MESSAGE_CONTRACT_SIGHTSEEING_TOUR_END_LOCATION_DESC
				days = 30
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = SYSTEM
					scope = event_target:sightseeing_tour_end_system
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.3065.a
		custom_tooltip = nomads.3060.a.tt
	}
}

# Sightseeing Tour - Check if Arkship has entered the system to drop off tourists
# Fired by: on_entering_system_fleet
# A fleet has entered a system
# Scope = Fleet
# From = System
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3070
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_event_chain = contract_sightseeing_tour_chain
		}
		from = {
			has_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_end_system@root.owner
		}
		has_fleet_flag = sightseeing_tour_arkship
	}

	immediate = {
		remove_fleet_flag = sightseeing_tour_arkship
		from = {
			remove_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_end_system@root.owner
			remove_star_flag = sightseeing_tour_tourists_picked_upp@root.owner
		}
		owner = {
			remove_point_of_interest = sightseeing_tour_destination_poi
			add_mission_counter = {
				mission = contract_sightseeing_tour
				counter = contract_progress_counter
				amount = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # War with nomad mercs is won. Remove event chain and hired guns modifier
	id = nomads.3075
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		fromfrom = {
			has_war_flag = nomad_mercs
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		fromfrom = {
			every_war_participant = {
				limit = { # we check that they have the flag that connects them to this war and that they aren't involved in another war with the contract issuer
					has_country_flag = war@fromfrom
					NOT = {
						any_war = {
							NOT = { is_same_value = fromfrom }
							any_war_participant = {
								has_country_flag = hired_nomad_merc@prevprev
							}
						}
					}
				}
				end_event_chain = contract_join_war_chain
				#remove hired_gun modifier
				remove_modifier = hired_guns_modifier
				#clean up issuer flag
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = hired_nomad_merc@prev
					}
					remove_country_flag = hired_nomad_merc@prev
					remove_country_flag = join_war_contract_active
				}
			}
			every_war_participant = {#Clean up the flag related to the war that just ended
				remove_country_flag = war@fromfrom
			}
		}
	}
}

					limit = {
						has_country_flag = hired_nomad_merc@prev
					}
					remove_country_flag = hired_nomad_merc@prev
					remove_country_flag = join_war_contract_active
				}

# Hired guns upkeep reduction handler
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.3085
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		controller = {
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_hired_guns
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_hired_guns
			}
		}
		from.controller? = {
			is_hostile = root.controller
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		every_owned_ship = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_modifier = hg_ship_upkeep_bombing }
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = hg_ship_upkeep_bombing
				days = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

# Cancel unaccepted Join Wars contracts when the issuer's last war ends
# on_war_won: Root = Winner Warleader, From = Loser Warleader, FromFrom = War
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3100
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		fromfrom = {
			any_war_participant = {
				is_at_war = no
				any_issued_mission = {
					is_mission_type = contract_join_war
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		fromfrom = {
			every_war_participant = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_at_war = no }
					every_issued_mission = {
						limit = { is_mission_type = contract_join_war }
						cancel_contract = { refund = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Cancel unaccepted Join Wars contracts when the issuer's last war ends (white peace)
# on_status_quo: Root = Actor, From = Recipient, FromFrom = Main Attacker, FromFromFrom = Main Defender, FromFromFromFrom = War
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3101
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		fromfromfromfrom = {
			any_war_participant = {
				is_at_war = no
				any_issued_mission = {
					is_mission_type = contract_join_war
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		fromfromfromfrom = {
			every_war_participant = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_at_war = no }
					every_issued_mission = {
						limit = { is_mission_type = contract_join_war }
						cancel_contract = { refund = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Total wars only end in status quo, so the raid war goal's ark-seizing surrender path never runs.
# on_status_quo: Root = Actor, From = Recipient, FromFrom = Main Attacker, FromFromFrom = Main Defender, FromFromFromFrom = War
country_event = {
	id = nomads.3105
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		fromfromfromfrom = {
			is_total_war = yes
			any_war_participant = {
				is_nomadic = yes
				any_owned_fleet = {
					is_arkship_fleet = yes
					NOT = { is_controlled_by = owner }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		# Resolve the on_status_quo scope chain (see header) once into readable named targets.
		fromfrom = { save_event_target_as = total_war_main_attacker }
		fromfromfrom = { save_event_target_as = total_war_main_defender }
		fromfromfromfrom = { save_event_target_as = total_war }
		event_target:total_war = {
			# Defeated nomads forfeit their occupied arkships to the opposing war leader.
			every_defender = {
				limit = { is_nomadic = yes }
				total_war_seize_occupied_arks_effect = { WINNER = event_target:total_war_main_attacker }
			}
			every_attacker = {
				limit = { is_nomadic = yes }
				total_war_seize_occupied_arks_effect = { WINNER = event_target:total_war_main_defender }
			}
		}
	}
}

##############################
### Arkships Functionality ###
##############################

# Fired by on_arkship_deep_scan
planet_event = {
	id = nomads.4000
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes

	immediate = {
		from = {
			random_owned_ship = {
				save_event_target_as = arkship
			}
		}
		# If anything is not surveyed, survey it.
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_surveyed = {
					who = from.controller
					status = no
				}
			}
			set_surveyed = {
				surveyed = yes
				surveyor = from.controller
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_planet
			event_target:arkship = {
				fire_on_action = {
					on_action = on_survey_planet
					scopes = {
						from = event_target:target_planet
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			# Already surveyed: on_survey_planet won't fire, so call the Sensor Calibration
			# checklist event directly so progress still ticks for a fully-explored galaxy.
			save_event_target_as = target_planet
			event_target:arkship = {
				ship_event = {
					id = nomads.52
					scopes = {
						from = event_target:target_planet
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# Chance to find hidden stuff...
		if = {
			limit = {
				habitable_planet = no
				is_artificial = no
				NOR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable_damaged
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_tech_damaged
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_tech
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_seam
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_seam_damaged
					is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar
				}
				# check that the random list won't come up empty
				OR = {
					energy_candidate = yes
					mineral_candidate = yes
					physics_candidate = yes
					society_candidate = yes
					engineering_candidate = yes
					alloy_candidate = yes
					exotic_gas_candidate = yes
					rare_crystal_candidate = yes
					volatile_motes_candidate = yes
				}
			}
			arkship_deep_scan_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				habitable_planet_not_urban = yes
				event_target:arkship.leader? = {
					has_leader_flag = nomadic_naturalist
				}
			}
			life_in_motion_effect = yes
		}
		from.controller = {
			create_message = {
				type = TOAST_DEEP_SCAN_COMPLETE
				localization = TOAST_DEEP_SCAN_COMPLETE_DESC
				days = @toast_message_days
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = ARKSHIP
					scope = event_target:arkship
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = PLANET
					scope = root
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fired by on_harvest_resources
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.4100
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from = {
			every_owned_ship = {
				save_event_target_as = arkship
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_civilian = yes
				}
				root = {
					arkship_harvest_resources_effect = {
						DURATION = @logistic_harvest_resources_duration
						TARGET = event_target:arkship
						EFFECT = add_resource_to_local_stockpile
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				root = {
					arkship_harvest_resources_effect = {
						DURATION = @arkship_harvest_resources_duration
						TARGET = event_target:arkship.controller
						EFFECT = add_resource
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# Decrease opinion of system owner
		if = {
			limit = {
				exempt_from_harvest_resources_opinion_reduction_trigger = no
			}
			space_owner? = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = opinion_arkship_harvested_resources
					who = event_target:arkship.controller
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Track Resource Harvesting Checklist progress
# Fired by on_harvest_resources
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.4101
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		from = {
			is_arkship_fleet = yes
		}
		from.controller = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_country_flag = checklist_harvest_resources
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		# Gas Giant or Toxic World → Exotic Gases
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant
					is_planet_class = pc_toxic
				}
				from.controller = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = checklist_harvested_exotic_gases }
				}
			}
			from.controller = {
				set_country_flag = checklist_harvested_exotic_gases
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = NOMAD_CHECKLIST_HARVEST_RESOURCES
					counter = EXOTIC_GASES_HARVESTED
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		# Frozen World → Rare Crystals
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_planet_class = pc_frozen
				from.controller = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = checklist_harvested_rare_crystals }
				}
			}
			from.controller = {
				set_country_flag = checklist_harvested_rare_crystals
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = NOMAD_CHECKLIST_HARVEST_RESOURCES
					counter = RARE_CRYSTALS_HARVESTED
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		# Molten World → Volatile Motes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_planet_class = pc_molten
				from.controller = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = checklist_harvested_volatile_motes }
				}
			}
			from.controller = {
				set_country_flag = checklist_harvested_volatile_motes
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = NOMAD_CHECKLIST_HARVEST_RESOURCES
					counter = VOLATILE_MOTES_HARVESTED
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fired by on_arkship_subspace_image
system_event = {
	id = nomads.4300
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = yes
	immediate = {
		set_star_flag = subspace_image_completed
		from = {
			random_owned_ship = {
				save_event_target_as = arkship
			}
		}
		# Sensor Calibration: stars already surveyed before this subspace image won't
		# fire on_survey_planet below, so call nomads.52 directly for those so progress
		# still ticks in a fully-explored galaxy. Unsurveyed stars are handled by the
		# on_survey_planet chain fired in the loop below.
		every_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_star = yes
				is_surveyed = {
					who = from.controller
					status = yes
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_star
			event_target:arkship = {
				ship_event = {
					id = nomads.52
					scopes = {
						from = event_target:target_star
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# If anything is not surveyed, survey it.
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_system_planet = {
					is_surveyed = {
						who = from.controller
						status = no
					}
				}
			}
			every_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				is_surveyed = {
					who = from.controller
					status = no
				}
			}
			set_surveyed = {
				surveyed = yes
				surveyor = from.controller
			}
			save_event_target_as = target_planet
			event_target:arkship = {
				fire_on_action = {
					on_action = on_survey_planet
					scopes = {
						from = event_target:target_planet
					}
				}
			}
		}
		}
		# Find hidden stuff...
		every_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				habitable_planet = no
				is_artificial = no
				NOR = {
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_habitable_damaged
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_tech_damaged
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_tech
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_seam
					is_planet_class = pc_ringworld_seam_damaged
					is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar
				}
				# check that the random list won't come up empty
				OR = {
					energy_candidate = yes
					mineral_candidate = yes
					physics_candidate = yes
					society_candidate = yes
					engineering_candidate = yes
					alloy_candidate = yes
					exotic_gas_candidate = yes
					rare_crystal_candidate = yes
					volatile_motes_candidate = yes
				}
			}
			arkship_subspace_image_planet_effect = yes
		}
		every_system_planet = {
			limit = {
				habitable_planet_not_urban = yes
				event_target:arkship.leader? = {
					has_leader_flag = nomadic_naturalist
				}
			}
			life_in_motion_effect = yes
		}
		arkship_subspace_image_system_effect = yes

		from.controller = {
			create_message = {
				type = TOAST_SUBSPACE_IMAGE_COMPLETE
				localization = TOAST_SUBSPACE_IMAGE_COMPLETE_DESC
				days = @toast_message_days
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = ARKSHIP
					scope = event_target:arkship
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = SYSTEM
					scope = root
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fired by on_arkship_reprocess_planet
planet_event = {
	id = nomads.4400
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from = {
			every_owned_ship = {
				save_event_target_as = arkship
			}
		}
		arkship_planetary_reprocessor_effect = yes
		# Decrease opinion of system owner
		if = {
			limit = {
				exempt_from_harvest_resources_opinion_reduction_trigger = no
			}
			space_owner? = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = opinion_arkship_reprocess_planet
					who = event_target:arkship.controller
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Fired by on_arkship_stellar_ignition
# THIS = planet
# FROM = triggering fleet
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.4500
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_star = yes
			}
			arkship_stellar_ignition_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			arkship_protostar_effect = yes
		}
		apply_stellar_ignition_habitability_penalties = yes
		from = {
			random_owned_ship = {
				save_event_target_as = arkship
			}
		}
		from.controller = {
			create_message = {
				type = TOAST_STELLAR_IGNITION_COMPLETE
				localization = TOAST_STELLAR_IGNITION_COMPLETE_DESC
				days = @toast_message_days
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = ARKSHIP
					scope = event_target:arkship
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = PLANET
					scope = root
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board"
						is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative"
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = resolution_breached_terraformed days = 3600 }
			}
			save_event_target_as = nomad_country
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_event_chain = contract_stellar_ignition_chain
					root = {
						has_planet_flag = stellar_ignition_planet@event_target:nomad_country
					}
				}
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = contract_stellar_ignition
					counter = contract_progress_counter
					amount = 1
				}
				set_country_flag = successful_stellar_ignition@root.solar_system
			}
		}
	}
}

## Fired by on_fleet_arkship_exodus_jump
# THIS = Fleet
# FROM = System jumping to
# FROMFROM = System jumped from
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.4650
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_owned_ship = {
			save_event_target_as = arkship
		}
		fromfrom = {
			every_fleet_in_system = {
				limit = {
					is_mobile = yes
					controller = {
						is_same_value = root.controller
					}
				}
				remove_auto_move_target = yes
				set_location = {
					target = event_target:arkship
					distance = 20
					angle = random
					direction = in_system
				}
			}
		}
		controller = {
			create_message = {
				type = TOAST_EXODUS_JUMP_COMPLETE
				localization = TOAST_EXODUS_JUMP_COMPLETE_DESC
				days = @toast_message_days
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = ARKSHIP
					scope = event_target:arkship
				}
				variable = {
					type = name
					localization = SYSTEM
					scope = from
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			arkship_exodus_jump_system_effects = yes
		}
	}
}

# THIS = planet
# FROM = triggering fleet
# Fired by on_arkship_settle
planet_event = {
	id = nomads.4700
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_timed_carrier_flag = {
			flag = nomad_recently_settled_flag
			days = 30
		}
		save_event_target_as = settled_planet
		solar_system = {
			# Block rival outposts and pre-FTL emergence while the Settle dialog is open.
			set_timed_star_flag = {
				flag = nomad_settling_in_progress
				days = 30
			}
			save_event_target_as = settled_system
		}
		from = {
			random_owned_ship = {
				limit = {
					is_colony = yes
				}
				save_event_target_as = settling_arkship
			}
		}
		from.owner = {
			save_event_target_as = player_country
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.4705
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = nomads.4705
	title = nomads.4705.name

	desc = {	# Regular empire
		text = nomads.4705.desc.regular
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
				is_machine_empire = yes
				has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
			}
		}
	}

	desc = { 	# Machine Intelligence
		text = nomads.4705.desc.machine
		trigger = {
			is_machine_empire = yes
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_forever_cruise }
		}
	}

	desc = { 	# Hive Mind
		text = nomads.4705.desc.hive
		trigger = {
			is_hive_empire = yes
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_forever_cruise }
		}
	}

	desc = {	# Regular empire Forever Cruise
		text = nomads.1010.regular.desc
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				is_hive_empire = yes
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
			has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		}
	}

	desc = {	# Hive Mind Forever Cruise
		text = nomads.1010.hive.desc
		trigger = {
			is_hive_empire = yes
			has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		}
	}

	desc = {	# Machine Intelligence Forever Cruise
		text = nomads.1010.machine.desc
		trigger = {
			is_machine_empire = yes
			has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		}
	}

	inline_script = {
		script = events/biogenesis_event_art
		OWNER = owner
		REGULAR_PICTURE = GFX_evt_big_landing_ship
		BIOSHIP_PICTURE = GFX_evt_bioship_landing
	}

	location = from
	is_triggered_only = yes

	# We only have one Arkship, and thus we Settle.
	option = {
		exclusive_trigger = {
			count_owned_ship = {
				count = 1
				limit = { is_arkship_ship = yes }
			}
		}
		name = nomads.4700.a
		custom_tooltip = nomads.4700.settle.tt
		arkship_settle_planet_effect = {
			SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			SETTLING_ARKSHIP = event_target:settling_arkship
			SETTLED_PLANET = event_target:settled_planet
			SETTLED_SYSTEM = event_target:settled_system
		}
		convert_waystations_into_outposts_effect = {
			SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
		}
		convert_logistic_ships_into_construction_ships_effects = yes
		custom_tooltip = convert_waystations_into_outposts_tt
		custom_tooltip = convert_logistics_to_construction_tt
	}

	# We have many Arkships, we Settle and scuttle them.
	option = {
		name = nomads.4700.b
		custom_tooltip = nomads.4700.settle.tt
		arkship_settle_planet_effect = {
			SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			SETTLING_ARKSHIP = event_target:settling_arkship
			SETTLED_PLANET = event_target:settled_planet
			SETTLED_SYSTEM = event_target:settled_system
		}
		convert_waystations_into_outposts_effect = {
			SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
		}
		settlement_scuttle_arkships_effect = {
			SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			SETTLED_PLANET = event_target:settled_planet
			SETTLING_ARKSHIP = event_target:settling_arkship
		}
		convert_logistic_ships_into_construction_ships_effects = yes
		custom_tooltip = settlement_scuttle_arkships_effect_tt
		custom_tooltip = convert_waystations_into_outposts_tt
		custom_tooltip = convert_logistics_to_construction_tt
	}

	# We have many Arkships, we stay Nomadic and release a Settled Subject.
	option = {
		trigger = {		# You need to be able to release a subject to have this option
			is_homicidal = no
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_origin = origin_progenitor_hive
			}
		}
		name = nomads.4700.c
		custom_tooltip = nomads.4700.settle_subject.tt
		create_settlement_subject_country_effect = {
			NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
		}
		tooltip = {
			event_target:settled_planet = {
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = arkship_parts
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = event_target:subject_country
			}
			arkship_settle_planet_effect = {
				SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:subject_country
				SETTLING_ARKSHIP = event_target:settling_arkship
				SETTLED_PLANET = event_target:settled_planet
				SETTLED_SYSTEM = event_target:settled_system
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				give_planet_and_system_to_rebel = {
					PLANET = event_target:settled_planet
					REBEL = event_target:subject_country
					OLD_OWNER = event_target:player_country
				}
			}
			event_target:subject_country? = {
				clean_up_settlement_subject_country_effect = {
					OVERLORD = event_target:player_country
				}
				set_origin_effect = { SOURCE_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_origin = origin_default
					}
					set_origin = origin_nomadic_settled
				}
			}
			create_outposts_in_waystation_systems_effect = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:subject_country
				SETTLED_SYSTEM = event_target:settled_system
				RANGE = @arkship_subject_settle_outpost_range
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = create_outposts_in_waystation_systems_for_subject_tt
		# We keep our logistic ships as we stay Nomadic
	}

	# We have many Arkships, we Settle and release a Nomadic Subject.
	option = {
		trigger = {		# You need to be able to release a subject to have this option
			is_homicidal = no
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_origin = origin_progenitor_hive
			}
		}
		name = nomads.4700.d
		custom_tooltip = nomads.4700.settle.tt
		create_settlement_subject_country_effect = {
			NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
		}
		arkship_settle_planet_effect = {
			SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			SETTLING_ARKSHIP = event_target:settling_arkship
			SETTLED_PLANET = event_target:settled_planet
			SETTLED_SYSTEM = event_target:settled_system
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = event_target:subject_country
			}
			nomad_give_arkships_to_subject_effect = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:subject_country
				SETTLING_ARKSHIP = event_target:settling_arkship
			}
			event_target:subject_country? = {
				set_country_as_nomad_effect = { IS_NOMAD = yes }
				set_faction_properties = {
					needs_border_access = no
				}
				set_resource_converter = nomadic_operational_reserves
				clean_up_settlement_subject_country_effect = {
					OVERLORD = event_target:player_country
				}
				set_origin_effect = { SOURCE_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_origin = origin_default
					}
					set_origin = origin_nomadic_subject
				}
			}
			create_outposts_in_waystation_systems_effect = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				SETTLED_SYSTEM = event_target:settled_system
				RANGE = @arkship_subject_settle_outpost_range
			}
			nomad_give_waystations_to_subject_effect = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:subject_country
				SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			}
			nomad_give_logistic_ships_to_subject_effect = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:subject_country
				SETTLING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = create_outposts_in_waystation_systems_for_overlord_tt
		custom_tooltip = make_subject_nomadic_tt
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_origin = origin_forever_cruise }
				remove_forever_cruise_citizenships = yes
				set_country_flag = forever_cruise_over
				random_situation = {
					limit = { is_situation_type = situation_passenger_satisfaction }
					destroy_situation = this
				}
				save_event_target_as = this_country
				country_event = { id = timeline.115 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

				EMBARKING_PLANET = from
			}
		}

				}

			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = create_waystations_in_systems_for_nomad_tt
	}

	# We are embarking as civilians.
	option = {
		name = nomads.4710.a.civilian
		custom_tooltip = nomads.4710.embark.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			create_embarking_arkship = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				ARKSHIP_TYPE = civilian
				EMBARKED_PLANET = from
			}
			embark_planet_effect = {
				EMBARKING_PLANET = from
				NEW_ARKSHIP = event_target:embarking_arkship
			}
			give_embarking_empire_logistic_ship = {
				EMBARKING_PLANET = from
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				count_owned_colony = {
					count > 1
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				create_embarking_subject_country_effect = {
					PLAYER_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				}
				last_created_country? = {
					save_event_target_as = subject_country
				}
				convert_starbases_into_waystation_effect = {
					PLAYER_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
					EMBARKING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				}
				every_owned_colony = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_planet_class = pc_ark }
					}
					set_owner = last_created_country
				}
				every_owned_fleet = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ship_size = constructor
							is_ship_size = engineer_vessel
						}
					}
					set_owner = last_created_country
				}
				every_owned_megastructure = {
					limit = { is_megastructure_incompatible_with_nomads = yes }
					set_owner = last_created_country
				}
				last_created_country? = {
					clean_up_settlement_subject_country_effect = {
						OVERLORD = event_target:player_country
					}
					set_origin_effect = { SOURCE_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country }
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = embark_leaves_behind_subject
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				convert_starbases_into_waystation_effect = {
					PLAYER_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
					EMBARKING_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				}
				every_owned_megastructure = {
					limit = { is_megastructure_incompatible_with_nomads = yes }
					remove_megastructure = this
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = create_waystations_in_systems_for_nomad_tt
	}

	# Our vassal is embarking.
	option = {
		trigger = {
			count_owned_colony = {
				count > 1
			}
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = no
				has_origin = origin_progenitor_hive
			}
		}
		name = nomads.4710.b
		hidden_effect = {
			create_embarking_subject_country_effect = {
				PLAYER_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
			}
			create_embarking_arkship = {
				NOMAD_COUNTRY = last_created_country
				ARKSHIP_TYPE = civilian
				EMBARKED_PLANET = from
			}
			from = {
				set_owner = last_created_country
				leader? = {
					unassign_leader = this
				}
			}

			embark_planet_effect = {
				EMBARKING_PLANET = from
				NEW_ARKSHIP = event_target:embarking_arkship
			}
			last_created_country? = {
				clean_up_settlement_subject_country_effect = {
					OVERLORD = event_target:player_country
				}
				set_origin_effect = { SOURCE_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country }
				give_embarking_empire_logistic_ship = { EMBARKING_PLANET = from }
			}
			last_created_country? = {
				save_event_target_as = subject_country
			}
			convert_starbases_into_waystation_effect = {
				PLAYER_COUNTRY = event_target:player_country
				EMBARKING_COUNTRY = event_target:subject_country
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = embark_create_subject
		custom_tooltip = create_waystations_in_systems_for_nomad_tt
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:embarking_arkship = {
				set_name = {
					key = NAME_Embarked_Arkship
					variable_string = "[From.GetName]"
				}
				fleet = {
					set_name = {
						key = NAME_Embarked_Arkship
						variable_string = "[From.GetName]"
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = embarking_from_doomsday
			}
			remove_country_flag = embarking_from_doomsday
			if = {
				limit = { has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness }
				capital_scope = {
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = doomsday_first_arkship_gestalt
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				capital_scope = {
					add_modifier = {
						modifier = doomsday_first_arkship
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Scope = Ship
# From = System
# FromFrom = Country
ship_event = { # Nomad Exploration Rewards
	id = nomads.4720
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			has_ascension_perk = ap_wanderlust
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nomad_exploration_complete
			}
		}
		is_arkship_ship = yes
		from = {
			NOT = { has_star_flag = visited_by_nomad@root.owner }
			#Flags Check
			OR = {
				has_star_flag = ancient_wonders_system
				has_star_flag = antique_threat_system
				has_star_flag = enclave
				has_star_flag = galactic_landmark_system
				has_star_flag = marauder_system
				has_star_flag = natural_spectacle_system
				has_star_flag = precursor_system
				has_star_flag = space_ecology_system
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		from = {
			set_star_flag = visited_by_nomad@root.owner
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				from = { has_star_flag = curator_guidance_target@root.owner }
			}
			from = { remove_star_flag = curator_guidance_target@root.owner }
			owner = { remove_point_of_interest = curator_guidance_poi@from }
		}
		if = { #failsafe check for event chain
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owner = { has_event_chain = nomad_exploration_chain }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				begin_event_chain = {
					event_chain = nomad_exploration_chain
					target = this
				}
			}
		}
		#increment the counters and update the modifiers,
		if = {
			limit = {
				from = { has_star_flag = ancient_wonders_system }
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = ancient_wonders_system_seen
					value = 1
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = ancient_wonders_modifier
					mult = value:ancient_wonders_system_ratio
					days = -1
				}
				if = { #if category is finished, give flag for arkship size
					limit = {
						check_variable_arithmetic = {
							which = value:ancient_wonders_system_ratio
							multiply = 1
							value >= 1
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = ancient_wonders_completed
						}
					}
					add_mission_counter = {
						mission = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ANCIENT_WONDERS
						counter = ancient_wonders_progress
						amount = 1
					}
				}
				#notify
				create_message = {
					type = NOMAD_EXPLORATION
					localization = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_WONDERS_DESC
					days = 20
					target = from
					variable = {
						type = name
						localization = SYSTEM
						scope = from
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				from = { has_star_flag = antique_threat_system }
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = antique_threat_system_seen
					value = 1
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = antique_threat_modifier
					mult = value:antique_threat_system_ratio
					days = -1
				}
				if = { #if category is finished, give flag for arkship size
					limit = {
						check_variable_arithmetic = {
							which = value:antique_threat_system_ratio
							multiply = 1
							value >= 1
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = antique_threat_completed
						}
					}
					add_mission_counter = {
						mission = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ANTIQUE_THREAT
						counter = antique_threat_progress
						amount = 1
					}
				}
				#notify
				create_message = {
					type = NOMAD_EXPLORATION
					localization = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_THREAT_DESC
					days = 20
					target = from
					variable = {
						type = name
						localization = SYSTEM
						scope = from
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				from = { has_star_flag = enclave }
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = enclave_system_seen
					value = 1
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = enclave_modifier
					mult = value:enclave_system_ratio
					days = -1
				}
				if = { #if category is finished, give flag for arkship size
					limit = {
						check_variable_arithmetic = {
							which = value:enclave_system_ratio
							multiply = 1
							value >= 1
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = enclave_completed
						}
					}
					add_mission_counter = {
						mission = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ENCLAVE
						counter = enclave_progress
						amount = 1
					}
				}
				#notify

					target = from

		}

					}

		if = {

					}
				}
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = space_ecology_completed } }
			}
			owner = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_SPACE_ECOLOGY
					counter = space_ecology_progress
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_system = {
						has_star_flag = enclave
					}
				}
				NOT = { owner = { has_country_flag = enclave_completed } }
			}
			owner = {
				add_mission_counter = {
					mission = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ENCLAVE
					counter = enclave_progress
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}
		# grant small unity reward and notify
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1unityreward
				min = @tier1unitymin
				max = @tier1unitymax
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Nomad Exploration Intro
	id = nomads.4715
	title = "nomads.4715.name"
	desc = "nomads.4715.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_tiyanki_observation
	show_sound = relic_activation_the_surveyor

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# exploration trackers - set here (rather than on becoming nomadic) so
		# that mid-game nomad creation paths (GRS spawn, mid-game embark,
		# settlement subjects) are also covered the moment they pick the perk
		calculate_nomads_exploration_targets = yes
		setup_nomad_exploration_trackers = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.4715.a
		trigger = { owner = { is_xenophobe = no } }
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.4715.b
		trigger = { owner = { is_xenophobe = yes } }

	}

	after = {
		begin_event_chain = {
			event_chain = nomad_exploration_chain
			target = this
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ANCIENT_WONDERS
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ANTIQUE_THREAT
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_ENCLAVE
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_GALACTIC_LANDMARK
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_MARAUDER
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_NATURAL_SPECTACLE
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_PRECURSOR
		}
		enable_mission = {
			name = NOMAD_EXPLORATION_SPACE_ECOLOGY
		}
	}
}

# Fired by on_arkship_lithoid_consume_world (on_progress_start)
# Starts the consume situation on first arrival, or resumes it if the fleet returns after cancelling.
# THIS = planet
# FROM = triggering fleet
planet_event = {
	id = nomads.4750
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_carrier_flag = being_devoured } }
			# First arrival: full initialisation
			set_timed_carrier_flag = {
				days = 360
				flag = recently_eaten_planet
			}
			set_carrier_flag = colony_event
			set_carrier_flag = being_devoured
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = being_devoured_modifier
				days = -1
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = planet_size
				variable = num_districts_terravore
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = count_deposits
				parameters = {
					type = d_lithoid_devastation
				}
				variable = num_lithoid_blockers
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_variable_set = num_lithoid_blockers
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = num_districts_terravore
					value = num_lithoid_blockers
				}
			}
			from.controller = {
				start_situation = {
					type = situation_arkship_lithoid_consume_planet
					target = root
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			# Returning after cancellation: clear the grace period flag
			remove_carrier_flag = arkship_absent_grace
		}
		from = { set_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root }
	}
}

# Arkship Lithoid Consume Planet - Monthly
# Delivers resources when the consuming arkship is present (grace flag not active).
# THIS = situation, owner = consuming empire, target = planet
situation_event = {
	id = nomads.4755
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# Consume tick: only when arkship is present and not on cooldown
		if = {
			limit = {
				target = {
					NOR = {
						has_carrier_flag = recently_eaten_planet
						has_carrier_flag = arkship_absent_grace
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = { # Pop: new bodies absorbed into the arkship colony
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						target = { num_free_districts = { type = any value < 2 } }
					}
					target = {
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_planet_devastation = 20
					}
					owner = {
						random_owned_planet = {
							limit = {
								is_colony = yes
								ship = { fleet = { has_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root.target } }
							}
							create_pop_group = { species = root.owner.owner_main_species }
						}
						create_message = {
							type = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD
							localization = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD_POP_TEXT
							days = 30
							target = root.target
							variable = { type = name localization = PLANET scope = root.target }
						}
					}
				}
				10 = { # Minerals
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						target = { num_free_districts = { type = any value < 2 } }
					}
					target = {
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_planet_devastation = 20
					}
					owner = {
						random_list = {
							1 = {
								add_resource = {
									minerals = 500
								}
							}
							1 = {
								add_resource = {
									minerals = 1000
								}
							}
							1 = {
								add_resource = {
									minerals = 3000
								}
							}
						}
						create_message = {
							type = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD
							localization = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD_MINERALS_TEXT
							days = 30
							target = root.target
							variable = { type = name localization = PLANET scope = root.target }
						}
					}
				}
				10 = { # Food
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						target = { num_free_districts = { type = any value < 2 } }
					}
					target = {
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_planet_devastation = 20
					}
					owner = {
						add_monthly_resource_mult = {
							resource = food
							value = 3
							min = @tier2materialmin
							max = @tier2materialmax
						}
						create_message = {
							type = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD
							localization = MESSAGE_ARKSHIP_LITHOID_CONSUME_WORLD_FOOD_TEXT
							days = 30
							target = root.target
							variable = { type = name localization = PLANET scope = root.target }
						}
					}
				}
				10 = { # Last slot - reduced yield
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						target = { num_free_districts = { type = any value >= 2 } }
					}
					target = {
						add_deposit = d_lithoid_devastation
						add_planet_devastation = 10
					}
					owner = {
						random_list = {
							1 = {
								add_resource = {
									minerals = 250
								}
							}
							1 = {
								add_resource = {
									minerals = 500
								}
							}
							1 = {
								add_resource = {
									minerals = 1500
								}
							}
						}
						create_message = {
							type = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD
							localization = MESSAGE_TERRAVORE_CONSUME_WORLD_MINERALS_TEXT
							days = 30
							target = root.target
							variable = { type = name localization = PLANET scope = root.target }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			target = {
				set_timed_carrier_flag = { flag = recently_eaten_planet days = 360 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Arkship Lithoid Consume Planet - Complete
# THIS = situation, owner = consuming empire, target = planet
situation_event = {
	id = nomads.4760
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis }
				complete_crisis_objective = crisobj_destroy_worlds
			}
			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = { has_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root.target }
				remove_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root.target
				save_event_target_as = devouring_fleet
			}
			create_message = {
				type = MESSAGE_LITHOID_CONSUME_WORLD_COMPLETE
				localization = TOAST_LITHOID_CONSUME_WORLD_COMPLETE_DESC
				days = 30
				target = root.target
				variable = { type = name localization = PLANET scope = root.target }
				variable = { type = name localization = ARKSHIP scope = event_target:devouring_fleet }
			}
		}
		target = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_modifier = holy_planet }
				carrier_event = { id = planet_destruction.605 scopes = { fromfrom = event_target:devouring_fleet } }
			}
			change_pc = pc_shattered
			clear_deposits = yes
			remove_carrier_flag = being_devoured
			remove_carrier_flag = colony_event
			remove_carrier_flag = arkship_absent_grace
			remove_modifier = being_devoured_modifier
		}
		destroy_situation = this
	}
}

# Fired by on_arkship_nanotech_consume_world (on_progress_start)
# Starts the consume situation on first arrival, or resumes it if the fleet returns after cancelling.
# THIS = planet
# FROM = triggering fleet
planet_event = {
	id = nomads.4800
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_carrier_flag = being_devoured } }
			# First arrival: full initialisation
			set_timed_carrier_flag = {
				days = 360
				flag = recently_eaten_planet
			}
			set_carrier_flag = colony_event
			set_carrier_flag = being_devoured
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = being_devoured_modifier_nanotech
				days = -1
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = planet_size
				variable = num_districts_terravore
			}
			export_trigger_value_to_variable = {
				trigger = count_deposits
				parameters = {
					type = d_nanotech_devastation
				}
				variable = num_lithoid_blockers
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_variable_set = num_lithoid_blockers
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = num_districts_terravore
					value = num_lithoid_blockers
				}
			}
			from.controller = {
				start_situation = {
					type = situation_arkship_nanotech_consume_planet
					target = root
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			# Returning after cancellation: clear the grace period flag
			remove_carrier_flag = arkship_absent_grace
		}
		from = { set_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root }
	}
}

# Arkship Nanotech Consume Planet - Complete
# THIS = situation, owner = consuming empire, target = planet
situation_event = {
	id = nomads.4810
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		target = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_carrier_flag = fallen_empire_capital }
				owner = { set_country_flag = past_the_expiration_date_achievement }
			}
			change_pc = pc_gray_goo
			clear_deposits = yes
			add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit_regular
				}
				5 = {
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit_regular
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit
				}
				5 = {
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit_regular
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit_regular
				}
				1 = {
					add_deposit = d_nanite_harvester_deposit_large
				}
			}
			remove_carrier_flag = being_devoured
			remove_carrier_flag = colony_event
			remove_carrier_flag = arkship_absent_grace
			remove_modifier = being_devoured_modifier_nanotech
			carrier_event = { id = action.68 }
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = nanotech_consuming_empire
			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = { has_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root.target }
				remove_fleet_flag = consuming_world_arkship@root.target
				save_event_target_as = consuming_fleet
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = nanotech_worlds_created
				value = 1
			}
			create_message = {
				type = MESSAGE_NANOTECH_CONSUME_WORLD_COMPLETE
				localization = TOAST_NANOTECH_CONSUME_WORLD_COMPLETE_DESC
				days = 30
				target = root.target
				variable = { type = name localization = PLANET scope = root.target }
				variable = { type = name localization = ARKSHIP scope = event_target:consuming_fleet }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_nomadic = no
				NOT = { is_same_value = event_target:nanotech_consuming_empire }
				has_communications = event_target:nanotech_consuming_empire
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_arkship_nanotech_consume_world
				who = event_target:nanotech_consuming_empire
			}
		}
		destroy_situation = this
	}
}

#Reavers plunder resources while bombing a planet - FROM = Bombarder
carrier_event = {
	id = nomads.5005
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_carrier_flag = recently_plundered }
		has_orbital_bombardment_stance = plundering
		planet_devastation <= 70
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "booty plundered"
		set_timed_carrier_flag = {
			flag = recently_plundered
			days = 30
		}
		random_list = {
			2.5 = { #No Booty
				#  Increased by armies on the planet
				modifier = {
					factor = trigger:num_armies
				}
			}
			50 = { #Steal 40% of a month of prod
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.1
					any_fleet_in_orbit = {
						controller = {
							is_same_value = from
						}
						leader? = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_plunderer
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.15
					any_fleet_in_orbit = {
						controller = {
							is_same_value = from
						}
						leader? = {
							has_trait = leader_trait_plunderer_2
						}
					}
				}
				steal_planet_output = {
					planet = this
					who = FROM
					resource = all
					percentage = 0.4
					mode = steal
					notification_mode = both
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

starbase_event = {
	id = nomads.5010
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		# waystation still exists and still has module
		exists = root
		solar_system = {
			any_fleet_in_system = {
				is_waystation_ship = yes
				starbase = {
					has_starbase_module = waystation_pirate_hideout
				}
			}
		}
		NOR = {
			has_starbase_flag = piracy_collected
			solar_system = {
				space_owner = { is_same_value = root.owner }
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_timed_starbase_flag = {
			flag = piracy_collected
			days = 29
		}
		if = {
			limit = { root.fleet = { is_cloaked = no } }
			solar_system = {
				every_system_planet = {
					limit = { is_colony = yes }
					owner = {
						add_opinion_modifier = {
							who = root.owner
							modifier = opinion_waystation_piracy
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		starbase_event = { id = nomads.5010 days = 30 }
	}
}
## Add and remove Deep Sleep blockers for loser (on_war_ended)
country_event = {
	id = nomads.5020
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		any_owned_colony = {
			NOR = {
				has_deposit = d_deep_sleep_cryo_pods
				has_deposit = d_deep_sleep_cryo_pods_renewed
			}
		}
		is_deep_sleep_country = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		every_owned_colony = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_deposit = d_deep_sleep_cryo_pods
					has_deposit = d_deep_sleep_cryo_pods_renewed
				}
			}
			while = {
				count < 3
				add_deposit = d_deep_sleep_cryo_pods
			}
		}
	}
}

	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		owner? = {
			is_nomadic = yes
		}
	}

			}
			spread_tent_ships_tier_1 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_arkship_tier_2 = yes
			}
			spread_tent_ships_tier_2 = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_arkship_tier_3 = yes
			}
			spread_tent_ships_tier_3 = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Delayed cleanup: removes contract_downtime_taken after the contract completion popup has been built
	id = nomads.6998
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		remove_country_flag = contract_downtime_taken
	}
}

country_event = { #Contract event gatekeeper
	id = nomads.6000
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = no_contract_event_allowed
		}
		exists = fromfrom
	}

	immediate = {
		#roll event chance
		random_list = {
			18 = {
				modifier = {
					has_country_flag = recent_contract_event_check
					factor = 10
				}
			}
			2 = {
				#save_event_targets
				fromfrom = {
					save_event_target_as = contract_issuer
				}
				fromfromfrom = {
					save_event_target_as = contract_system
				}
				random_owned_contract = {
					limit = {
						issuer = {
							is_same_value = event_target:contract_issuer
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = ongoing_contract
				}
				#roll event type
				random_list = { #We use an on_action to simplify filtering by contract category
					70 = { fire_on_action = { on_action = on_contract_event_common } } #70
					25 = { fire_on_action = { on_action = on_contract_event_rare } } #25
					5 = { fire_on_action = { on_action = on_contract_event_unique } } #5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = recent_contract_event_check days = 360 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Global Rare 1/5 - Arkship Equipment Breaks :c
	id = nomads.6015
	title = "nomads.6015.name"
	desc = "nomads.6015.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_nomad_default
	show_sound = event_arkship_in_crisis

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		#owned arkship has four modules
		any_owned_fleet = {
			starbase? = {
				is_arkship_starbase = yes
				count_starbase_modules = {
					include_being_constructed = no
					count >= 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		#save the target
		random_owned_fleet = {
			limit = {
				starbase? = {
					is_arkship_starbase = yes
					count_starbase_modules = {
						include_being_constructed = no
						count >= 3
					}
				}
			}
			starbase = {
				save_event_target_as = target_arkship
				colony = {
					save_event_target_as = arkship_colony
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Fix em
		name = nomads.6015.a
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_scavengers
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_scavengers
			}
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value >= 200
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			alloys = -200
		}
	}

	option = { #let them break
		name = nomads.6015.b
		while = {
			count = 3
			event_target:target_arkship = {
				remove_starbase_module = {
					slot = all
					module = all
				}
			}
		}
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = module_recycling
			days = 720
		}
	}

	option = { #Perhaps an upgrade - gain an extra arkship district
		name = nomads.6015.c
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value >= 500
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			alloys = -500
		}
		event_target:arkship_colony = {
			add_deposit = d_compact_modules
		}
	}

	option = { #Scavengers fix it for almost free and get unity
		name = nomads.6015.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_scavengers
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_scavengers
			}
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value >= 50
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			alloys = -50
			unity = 500
		}
	}

	option = { # Charge the contract issuer instead
		name = nomads.6015.e
		trigger = {
			is_megacorp = no
		}
		custom_tooltip = nomads.6015.e.tt
		#Contract issuer loses opinion
		event_target:contract_issuer = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_abused_contract
				who = root
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Charge the contract issuer - Megacorp
		name = nomads.6015.e
		trigger = {
			is_megacorp = yes
		}
		custom_tooltip = nomads.6015.e.tt
		add_resource = {
			trade = 150
		}
		#Contract issuer loses more opinion
		event_target:contract_issuer = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_abused_contract_2
				who = root
			}
		}
	}
}

# Unexpected Cargo - Event Chain
country_event = {
	id = nomads.6020
	title = "nomads.6020.name"
	desc = "nomads.6020.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_nomad_default
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		is_nomadic = yes
		is_gestalt = no
		has_contract_of_category = resource_contract
		NOT = { has_country_flag = unexpected_cargo_flag }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = unexpected_cargo_flag
		}
	}

	option = { #Discard
		name = nomads.6020.a
		#fail ongoing contract, reward with unity because we are protecting the crew
		event_target:contract_issuer = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_unexpected_cargo_negative
				who = root.owner
			}
		}
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1unityreward
				min = @tier1unitymin
				max = @tier1unitymax
			}
		}
		event_target:ongoing_contract = {
			cancel_contract = {
				refund = no
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Check up on the noises, will give a random chance
		name = nomads.6020.b
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { # bioluminescent critters
					country_event = { id = nomads.6025 days = 10 random = 20 } }
				1 = { # space kitten
					country_event = { id = nomads.6030 days = 10 random = 20 } }
				1 = { # mechanoid
					country_event = { id = nomads.6035 days = 10 random = 20 } }
				1 = { # minor explosions
					country_event = { id = nomads.6040 days = 10 random = 20 } }
				1 = { # leader
					country_event = { id = nomads.6045 days = 10 random = 20 } }
				1 = { # stowaways
					country_event = { id = nomads.6050 days = 10 random = 20 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # space kitten
	id = nomads.6030
	title = "nomads.6030.name"
	desc = "nomads.6030.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_but_they_are_cute
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_owned_leader = {
			limit = { is_ruler = no }
			save_event_target_as = cat_dad
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.6030.a
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = society_research
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax
			}
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = alloys
				value >= 100
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			alloys = -100
		}
	}

	option = { #give leader the pet trait, otherwise eager trait
		name = nomads.6030.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:cat_dad = {
					NOT = { has_trait = leader_trait_emotional_support_pet }
				}
			}
			event_target:cat_dad = {
				add_trait = {
					trait = leader_trait_emotional_support_pet
					show_message = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:cat_dad = {
					NOT = { has_trait = leader_trait_eager }
				}
			}
			event_target:cat_dad = {
				add_trait = {
					trait = leader_trait_eager
					show_message = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			event_target:cat_dad = {
				add_experience = 500
			}
		}
	}
}

			type = MESSAGE_RECRUITED_LEADER

			days = @toast_message_days
			target = event_target:arkship_cargo_leader
			variable = {
				type = name
				localization = LEADER
				scope = event_target:arkship_cargo_leader
			}
			variable = {
				key = "border"
				value = "GFX_invisible"
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.6045.b
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = alloys
				value = @tier2materialreward
				min = @tier2materialmin
				max = @tier2materialmax
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_devouring_swarm

				has_valid_civic = civic_fanatic_purifiers
				has_ascension_perk = ap_nihilistic_acquisition
				has_policy_flag = slavery_allowed
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_owned_colony = {
			save_event_target_as = arkship_colony
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.6050.a
		event_target:contract_issuer = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_unexpected_cargo_positive
				who = root.owner
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.6050.b
		owner = {
			add_intel = {
				amount = 30
				who = event_target:contract_issuer
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.6050.c
		event_target:arkship_colony = {
			create_pop_group = {
				species = event_target:contract_issuer.species
				size = 50
			}
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = consumer_goods
				value >= 500
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			consumer_goods = -500
		}
	}
}

############
#Migration##
############

country_event = {
	id = nomads.7000
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_homicidal = no
		is_country_type = default
		has_encountered_other_species = yes
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_ethic = "ethic_gestalt_consciousness" }
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		}
		any_owned_fleet = {
			is_arkship_ship = yes
			solar_system? = {
				any_system_planet_colony = {
					can_receive_nomad_migration = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = migration_information
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = nomads.7005
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_policy_flag = refugees_allowed }
			random_owned_fleet = {
				limit = {
					is_arkship_ship = yes
					solar_system? = {
						any_system_planet_colony = {
							can_receive_nomad_migration = yes
						}
					}
				}
				random_owned_ship = {
					limit = { is_arkship_ship = yes }
					save_event_target_as = migrating_arkship
				}
				solar_system = {
					random_system_planet = {
						limit = {
							can_receive_nomad_migration = yes
						}
						save_event_target_as = migrating_planet
					}
				}
				owner = {
					arkship_migration_effect = yes
				}
			}
			# Player toast — at most once per year, regardless of how many migrations fired
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = nomad_migration_toast_recent } }
				set_timed_country_flag = {
					flag = nomad_migration_toast_recent
					years = 1
				}
				create_message = {
					type = MESSAGE_NOMAD_MIGRATION
					localization = MESSAGE_NOMAD_MIGRATION_DESC
					days = 30
					target = event_target:migrating_planet
					variable = {
						type = name
						localization = PLANET
						scope = event_target:migrating_planet
					}
					variable = {
						type = name
						localization = ARKSHIP
						scope = event_target:migrating_arkship
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = nomads.7005
	title = "nomads.7005.title"

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_origin = origin_forever_cruise }
		text = "nomads.7005.desc.forever_cruise"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_origin = origin_forever_cruise }
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
		}
		text = "nomads.7005.desc.servitor"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			}
			event_target:migrating_planet = {
				owner = { is_same_species = root }
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.7005.desc.same_species"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
				event_target:migrating_planet = {
					owner = { is_same_species = root }
				}
			}
		}
		text = "nomads.7005.desc"
	}

	picture = GFX_evt_nomad_default
	show_sound = event_ambient_arkship_engine
	is_triggered_only = yes
	location = event_target:migrating_planet

	trigger = {
		# Must be able to set a Refugee Policy
		has_encountered_other_species = yes
		is_country_type = default
		is_homicidal = no
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_ethic = "ethic_gestalt_consciousness" }
			has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
			has_origin = origin_forever_cruise
		}
		any_owned_fleet = {
			is_arkship_ship = yes
			solar_system? = {
				any_system_planet_colony = {
					can_receive_nomad_migration = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = migration_information
		random_owned_fleet = {
			limit = {
				is_arkship_ship = yes
				solar_system? = {
					any_system_planet_colony = {
						can_receive_nomad_migration = yes
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_ship = {
				limit = { is_arkship_ship = yes }
				save_event_target_as = migrating_arkship
			}
			solar_system = {
				random_system_planet = {
					limit = {
						can_receive_nomad_migration = yes
					}
					save_event_target_as = migrating_planet
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.7005.a
		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = civic_tooltip_not_xenophobe
				is_xenophobe = no
			}
		}
		set_policy = {
			policy = refugees
			option = refugees_allowed
		}
		arkship_migration_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.7005.b
		arkship_migration_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = nomads.7005.c
		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = civic_tooltip_not_xenophile
				is_xenophile = no
			}
		}
		set_policy = {
			policy = refugees
			option = refugees_not_allowed
		}
	}
}

#Nomad Dyson Gun Impact
# THIS = Target System
# FROM = Megastructure
system_event = {
	id = nomads.8001
	hide_window = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		dyson_gun_impact_placement = yes
		# Warn the targeted system owner so they can move away before the cannon fires
		if = {
			limit = {
				space_owner? = {
					NOT = { is_same_value = from.owner }
				}
			}
			space_owner = {
				create_message = {
					type = MESSAGE_DYSON_TARGETED
					localization = MESSAGE_DYSON_TARGETED_DESC
					days = @toast_message_days
					target = root
					variable = {
						type = name
						localization = SYSTEM
						scope = root
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disable waystation in a nomad raid war
# THIS = Waystation Ship (taking damage)
# FROM = Attacking Ship
ship_event = {
	id = nomads.8004
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_disabled = no
		has_hp_percentage <= 0.5
		is_waystation_ship = yes
		exists = from
		from = { exists = owner }
		from = {
			owner = {
				any_war = {
					# Symmetric raid: either side may disable the other side's waystations
					OR = {
						any_defender = { is_same_value = root.owner }
						any_attacker = { is_same_value = root.owner }
					}
					OR = {
						using_war_goal = {
							type = wg_nomad_raid
							owner = prev
						}
						using_war_goal = {
							type = wg_raid_contract
							owner = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_disabled = yes
	}
}
