#8025 - steal station stockpile and choose to destroy it or not if nomad (regular automatically destroys)
country_event = {
	id = nomads.8025
	title = nomads.8025.name
	desc = nomads.8025.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_gunrunning
	show_sound = event_ground_battle
	location = event_target:target_waystation

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		event_target:target_waystation = {
			owner = {
				country_event = { id = nomads.8030 days = 3 }
			}
		}
		#roll for detection
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					has_tradition = tr_subterfuge_finish
					event_target:target_waystation.owner = {
						NOT = {
							has_tradition = tr_subterfuge_finish
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					event_target:target_waystation.owner = {
						relative_encryption_decryption = {
							target = root
							value < 1.0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					NOT = { has_tradition = tr_subterfuge_finish }
					event_target:target_waystation.owner = {
						has_tradition = tr_subterfuge_finish
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					relative_encryption_decryption = {
						target = event_target:target_waystation.owner
						value < 1.0
					}
				}
				from = { set_espionage_operation_flag = detected }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #destroy the station
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_espionage_asset_sabotage = yes
			}
		}
		name = nomads.8025.a
		custom_tooltip = nomads.8025.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:target_waystation = {
				fleet = {
					random_owned_ship = {
						transfer_resource_stockpile = {
							target = root
						}
					}
				}
				ship = {
					destroy_ship = this
				}
			}
		}
		from = {
			destroy_espionage_asset_sabotage = yes
			set_espionage_operation_flag = destroyed
		}
		from.spynetwork = {
			add_spy_network_level_on_success_effect = { VALUE = -75 }
		}
	}

	option = { #just loot it
		name = nomads.8025.b
		#destroy some modules
		event_target:target_waystation = {
			remove_starbase_module = {
				slot = 1
			}
		}
		from = { set_espionage_operation_flag = looted }
		from.spynetwork = {
			add_spy_network_level_on_success_effect = { VALUE = -35 }
		}
	}

	option = { #keep it
		trigger = {
			is_nomadic = yes
			from = {
				has_espionage_asset_manipulation = yes
			}
		}
		name = nomads.8025.c
		from = {
			destroy_espionage_asset_manipulation = yes
			set_espionage_operation_flag = stolen
		}
		#change ownership
		event_target:target_waystation = {
			set_owner = root
		}
		from.spynetwork = {
			add_spy_network_level_on_success_effect = { VALUE = -75 }
		}
	}

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = event_target:target_waystation }
			event_target:target_waystation = {
				fleet = {
					random_owned_ship = {
						transfer_resource_stockpile = {
							target = root
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = nomads.8030
	title = nomads.8030.name
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			fromfrom = {
				has_espionage_operation_flag = detected
				has_espionage_operation_flag = destroyed
			}
		}
		text = nomads.8030.detected_destroyed.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			fromfrom = {
				has_espionage_operation_flag = detected
				has_espionage_operation_flag = looted
			}
		}
		text = nomads.8030.detected_looted.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			fromfrom = {
				NOT = { has_espionage_operation_flag = detected }
				has_espionage_operation_flag = destroyed
			}
		}
		text = nomads.8030.destroyed.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			fromfrom = {
				NOT = { has_espionage_operation_flag = detected }
				has_espionage_operation_flag = looted
			}
		}
		text = nomads.8030.looted.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { fromfrom = { has_espionage_operation_flag = stolen } }
		text = nomads.8030.stolen.desc
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_guardians
	show_sound = event_ground_battle

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #tame option for looting cases
		trigger = {
			fromfrom = { has_espionage_operation_flag = looted }
		}
		name = UNFORTUNATE
		if = {
			limit = {
				fromfrom = {
					has_espionage_operation_flag = detected
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_waystation_looted_detected
				who = from
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #angry option for stealing and destroying
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				fromfrom = {
					has_espionage_operation_flag = destroyed
					has_espionage_operation_flag = stolen
				}
			}
		}
		name = CURSES
		if = {
			limit = {
				fromfrom = {
					OR = {
						has_espionage_operation_flag = detected
						has_espionage_operation_flag = stolen
					}
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = opinion_waystation_destroyed_detected
				who = from
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			destroy_espionage_operation = fromfrom
		}
	}
}


# nomads.8040 - Tribute Vault: clean up stale loyalty modifier for former subjects
country_event = {
	id = nomads.8040
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_modifier = tribute_vault_loyalty
		is_subject = no
	}

	immediate = {
		erase_modifier = { MOD = tribute_vault_loyalty }
		set_variable = { which = tribute_vault_count value = 0 }
	}
}

# Fired by on_starbase_destroyed
# This = starbase being destroyed (not ship!)
# From = fleet that destroyed the starbase
# nomads.8045 - Spawn debris when a disabled waystation is destroyed
# THIS = starbase (destroyed), FROM = destroying fleet
starbase_event = {
	id = nomads.8045
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_waystation_starbase = yes
		exists = from
		ship = { is_disabled = yes }
	}

	immediate = {
		fleet = {
			spawn_custom_debris = {
				for = from.owner
				reset_killed_ship_designs = yes
				reset_killed_ship_stockpile = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

### Clues of the Chrysanthemum

# A Voice from the Past
country_event = {
	id = nomads.9000
	title = "nomads.9000.name"
	desc = "nomads.9000.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_arkship_bridge
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter_02
	event_chain = clues_chrysanthemum

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
		has_country_flag = human_3
		any_system = {
			is_surveyed = {
				who = root
				status = no
			}
			distance = {
				source = root.capital_scope
				use_bypasses = no
				min_jumps = 1
				max_jumps = 5
			}
			NOT = { has_star_flag = hostile_system }
			has_owner = no
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		begin_event_chain = {
			event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
			target = ROOT
		}
		capital_scope.ship.fleet = {
			set_fleet_flag = hyacinth_fleet
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "nomads.9000.a"
		tooltip = {
			begin_event_chain = {
				event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_system = {
				limit = {
					is_surveyed = {
						who = root
						status = no
					}
					distance = {
						source = root.capital_scope
						use_bypasses = no
						min_jumps = 1
						max_jumps = 5
					}
					NOT = { has_star_flag = hostile_system }
					has_owner = no
				}
				save_event_target_as = chrysanthemum_relay_system
				set_star_flag = chrysanthemum_relay_system
			}
		}
		create_point_of_interest = {
			id = chrysanthemum_poi.1
			name = "chrysanthemum_poi_1"
			desc = "chrysanthemum_poi_1_desc"
			event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
			category = chrysanthemum_cat
			location = event_target:chrysanthemum_relay_system
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "nomads.9000.b"
		hidden_effect = {
			end_event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
		}
	}
}

# Signal Found
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.9005
	title = "nomads.9005.name"
	desc = "nomads.9005.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_star_chart
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = root
	event_chain = clues_chrysanthemum

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			has_event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
		}
		has_fleet_flag = hyacinth_fleet
		solar_system = { has_star_flag = chrysanthemum_relay_system }
	}

	immediate = {
		solar_system = { save_event_target_as = chrysanthemum_relay_system } # Just in case the player clicks the event option while they are in a hyper lane
	}

	option = {
		name = "nomads.9005.a"
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:chrysanthemum_relay_system = {
				remove_star_flag = chrysanthemum_relay_system
				random_neighbor_system = {
					weights = {
						base = 1
						modifier = { # For narative sake I would really like you not to end up back in Vela
							factor = 0.00001
							has_star_flag = vela_system
						}
					}
					spawn_system = {
						min_distance >= 10
						max_distance <= 30
						initializer = "chrysanthemum_tomb_system"
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				remove_point_of_interest = chrysanthemum_poi.1
				create_point_of_interest = {
					id = chrysanthemum_poi.2
					name = "chrysanthemum_poi_2"
					desc = "chrysanthemum_poi_2_desc"
					event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
					category = chrysanthemum_cat
					location = last_created_system
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Unity
fleet_event = {
	id = nomads.9010
	title = "nomads.9010.name"
	desc = "nomads.9010.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_arkship_in_orbit
	location = root
	trackable = yes
	event_chain = clues_chrysanthemum

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		owner? = {
			has_event_chain = "clues_chrysanthemum"
		}
		has_fleet_flag = hyacinth_fleet
		solar_system = { has_star_flag = chrysanthemum_tomb_system }
	}

	immediate = {
		owner = { remove_point_of_interest = chrysanthemum_poi.2 }
		solar_system = {
			remove_star_flag = chrysanthemum_tomb_system
			random_system_planet = {
				limit = { has_carrier_flag = unity_tomb }
				save_event_target_as = unity_planet
				create_ambient_object = {
					type = "chrysanthemum_object"
					location = THIS
				}
			}
		}
		last_created_ambient_object = {
			save_event_target_as = the_chrysanthemum
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "nomads.9010.a"
		event_target:unity_planet = {
			create_archaeological_site = site_chrysanthemum_colony
		}
	}
}

fleet_event = {	# The Escalation
	id = nomads.9015
	title = "nomads.9015.name"
	desc = "nomads.9015.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_tomb_world
	show_sound = event_dig_site
	location = from
	archaeology = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		from = { set_site_progress_locked = yes }
	}

	after = {
		from = { set_site_progress_locked = no }
	}

	option = {
		name = "nomads.9015.a"
		owner = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = unity
				value = @tier1unityreward
				min = @tier1unitymin
				max = @tier1unitymax
			}
		}
	}
}
